Important News

Recent Military News from the Pinghan Railway

▲Shi's Situation Is Isolated

▲The Situation on the Jinpu Railway Is Normal

Tianjin Correspondence: In recent days, due to the actions of Shi Yousan's troops, the situation here is changing from defensive to offensive. The pre-arranged military plan for the Pinghan Railway is that south of Shijiazhuang, there are no dangerous terrain to rely on, so the Northeast Army abandoned Shijiazhuang. Shi's vanguard is composed of the three divisions of Sun Guangqian, Shen Ke, and Sun Tielin. The troops that entered Shijiazhuang yesterday were part of Shen Ke's division. It is rumored that Shi Yousan himself has arrived in Gaoyi. Yu Xuezhong, the commander of the Northeast First Army, departed from Beiping the day before yesterday and arrived in Baoding yesterday. The headquarters is located in Guangyuan, commanding the Pinghan military operations. On the Jinpu Railway, passenger and freight trains have been running as usual in recent days. The Northeast previously stationed a brigade under Ding Xichun and a cavalry brigade under Li Fuhe in the northern section of the railway. Now, reinforcements have been added, and the strength is extremely abundant. Up to Sangyuan in the south, Wang Shuchang is still planning everything at the Deputy Commander's headquarters in Beiping because the situation has been stable recently. According to those familiar with military affairs, Shi's military actions were originally planned to coincide with those of Sun Dianying and others, but Sun and others have already declared their stance, supporting the central government. The Shanxi generals are especially obedient to Deputy Commander Zhang and are determined to remain loyal. Shi's situation has become isolated and is destined to fail without saying so. In Tianjin, fearing that reactionary elements would take the opportunity to act, martial law was declared the day before yesterday. Commander Zhang Xueming and Deputy Commander Guo Dianju have both arrived in Tianjin. The location is temporarily borrowed from the rear building of the Public Security Bureau as the office of the martial law headquarters, and Dong Peiqing has been appointed as the chief of the staff, Wu Yixian as the chief of the secretariat, Wang Yimin as the chief of the garrison, Sun Shaokang as the chief of the enforcement department, Lu Lu as the chief of the inspection department, and Tao Weiduo as the chief of the adjutant department. The content is divided into six departments, and most of the staff are concurrently filled by personnel from the Public Security Bureau. A notice has been issued saying, "Tianjin is a crucial hub connecting the north and south, and an important barrier for Hebei. With convenient transportation and people from all over the world residing here, local peace and stability are crucial to the overall situation. Currently, the situation is unstable, and rumors are rampant, easily causing panic. The citizens are affected by this. We have received instructions from the Deputy Commander of the Army, Navy, and Air Force Headquarters that Tianjin is a garrison area and that martial law will be implemented immediately. Zhang Xueming has been appointed as the Tianjin Martial Law Commander and Guo Dianju as the Deputy Martial Law Commander, and so on. Upon receiving these instructions, the Commander and Deputy Commander took office in Tianjin on the 22nd of this month. In accordance with the Martial Law Regulations, martial law is announced immediately. During the period of martial law, we will be responsible for the protection of local order, the lives and property of Chinese and foreign people, and the financial and commercial sectors, in order to maintain security. In addition to reporting and distributing this notice, we will detail the implementation measures in accordance with Article 9 of the Martial Law Regulations and announce them to the public. Therefore, we urge all soldiers and civilians to comply with this notice." (23rd)

Deputy Zhang's Representative Fan Pujiang Comes to Jinan Again

▲Hu Ruoyu, Jiang Bocheng, and Zhang Yue Also Arrive

▲Fan Talks About the Situation of Shi's Army and the Northeast Army

Jinan Correspondence: Fan Pujiang, representative of Zhang Xueliang, Jiang Bocheng, Chief Counselor of the General Headquarters of the Army, Navy, and Air Force, Zhang Yue, representative of Han Fuqu, arrived in Jinan at 9:45 AM today (23rd) on the Jinpu Railway. Hu Ruoyu, Mayor of Qingdao, also came on the same train. According to Jiang Bocheng, the situation in the north is very good. Deputy Commander Zhang, in order to ensure that the Commander-in-Chief can suppress the bandits in Jiangxi without worrying about the north, has decided to assume full responsibility for maintaining the overall situation in the north with Chairman Han. If anyone attempts to rebel, they will be eliminated in the shortest possible time. The Deputy Commander has fully recovered from his illness and took a photo with us in the hospital, showing his restored spirit. Fan Pujiang said that recently, because Yu Xuezhong, the Martial Law Commander of Beiping, went to the front to inspect defenses, he took over his duties. He had no time to come to Jinan, but Deputy Commander Zhang repeatedly sent him to thank Chairman Han (Fuqu), General Commander Ma (Hongkui), and Director Wang (Fangting) for sending people to Beiping to inquire about his health and to present gifts as a memento. The gifts for Ma included a complete set of Western silver tableware, a pair of cloisonné vases, a complete set of silver tea sets, a silk carpet (formerly from the Qing Palace collection), a complete set of Southern-style red lacquer stoves, and a set of single-lined robe and gown materials. The gifts for Han included a set of three blue and four-tube silver vases, and the rest were the same as the gifts for Ma. The gifts for Wang Fangting included an ivory carving of eight horses and single-lined robe and gown materials. Jiang Bocheng and Zhang Yue also received gifts. Deputy Commander Zhang and Chairman Han share the responsibility of maintaining the overall situation. Since Chief Counselor Jiang (Bocheng) and Committee Member Zhang (Yue) went to Beiping, their spirit has become more united. Zhang Yue said that the trip was a complete success. The Deputy Commander is determined to cooperate with Chairman Han to the end, and the overall situation in the north is optimistic. Hu Ruoyu said that he had no other mission here and planned to visit Chairman Han before returning to Qingdao. He will talk to everyone in detail when he has the opportunity. After Fan and others left the station, they went to the provincial government by car. Han immediately held a banquet to welcome them and invited Shao Lizi to join them. After the banquet, Hu Ruoyu took the Qingji Railway's military train to Qingdao.

After the banquet at the provincial government, reporters interviewed Fan Pujiang again. According to him, Chairman Han expressed his obedience to the General and Deputy Commanders, consistently and without wavering. Shi Yousan did not listen to Chairman Han's advice, and their friendship has ended. Although Shi still sends telegrams from time to time, Han sometimes ignores them and sometimes replies with a single character "悉" (xi, meaning "understood"), because Shi's rebellious attitude is clear and their personal positions are different. Shi Yousan's telegram to Beiping listed Sun Dianying's name, and Sun's representative in Beiping, Jin Zunhua, has declared on Sun's behalf that Shi fabricated and fabricated the information. The Shanxi generals obey the General and Deputy Commanders, and Fu Shuangying in Taiyuan is on extremely harmonious terms with them. Shi Yousan has arrived in Shijiazhuang, but is afraid to advance further because of the defense of Shanxi. The Northeast Army is now concentrating its troops on the Pinghan and Jinpu lines, waiting quietly. If Shi's army advances again, they will respond accordingly. He plans to go to Tai'an tomorrow (24th) to deliver gifts to General Commander Ma. Because the situation in Beiping is important, he will return to Beiping the day after tomorrow. (23rd)

New Appointments for Various Generals in Shandong Province

▲ Han Appointed Commander-in-Chief of the General Reserve Corps

▲ Ma, Sun, and Cao Appointed Commanders of Various Corps

Jinan Correspondence: After the Vice Commander-in-Chief of the Army, Navy, and Air Force, Shi Yousan, and others telegraphed their dissent, although there is still hope for their ultimate realization, preparations for a punitive expedition must be made to quell the rebellion in the shortest possible time. Furthermore, given the important strategic position of Shandong, it is essential to grant the generals stationed in Shandong appropriate titles to facilitate the command of various armies. Therefore, after consultation, Han Fuju was specially appointed as the Commander-in-Chief of the General Reserve Corps for the Suppression of Communists, Ma Hongkui as the Commander of the First Corps, Sun Tongxuan (Commander of the 20th Division) as the Commander of the Second Corps, and Cao Fulin (Commander of the 29th Division) as the Commander of the Third Corps. This order arrived in Jinan on the 22nd.

Previously, Han Fuju, due to military operations on the Pinghan Railway, had clearly demarcated the boundaries. To maintain public order in the province and prevent the intrusion of routed soldiers, he specially dispatched units from the Third and Fifteenth Routes to defend the borders of Shandong. The deployment is gradually nearing completion. Recently, our reporter visited Han, asking about the true situation of the current situation. According to him, Chief of General Staff Jiang (Bocheng) and Committee Member Zhang (Yue) returned to Jinan from Pingjin this morning, and the outcome was extremely satisfactory. Shi's forces are currently in the Shijiazhuang area, and the Jinpu Railway will certainly not experience any changes. The current troop movements in Shandong province are aimed at preventing defeated soldiers from entering the territory. He has always been a lover of peace and a protector of the region. However, since the founding of the Republic of China, internal wars have occurred countless times. If each war led to progress, it would be understandable. However, there has been no progress, and each result has been unfavorable. Even this war, in his opinion, is no different from an old farmer looking at a notice – the common people are destined for bad luck.

Han Fuju, in response to the skillful telegram sent by the Chairman of the Henan Provincial Government, Liu Zhi, and 33 other generals denouncing Shi Yousan, sent a reply on the 22nd. The original text is recorded below: "To Chief Commander Liu Jingfu of Kaifeng, Supervisor Liu Xueya of Luoyang, Supervisor Li Xiaodong of Guangshan, Chairman Yang Huchen of Xi'an, Chief Commander Gu Mosan of Zhengzhou, Commander Wang Zhiping of Lanfeng, Chief Commander Ji Shiwu of Guangshan, Chief Commander Liang Zichao of Qingjiang, Chief Commander Zhang Boying of Kaifeng, Chief Commander Liu Shulin of Luoyang, and forwarded to the Commanders of all armies and divisions. I recently received your skillful telegram, stating that with the communist atmosphere unrestrained and foreign aggression intensifying, all of us comrades should work together to uphold unity, save the country from destruction, and seek the survival of the nation. The words are solemn and the righteousness is upright, which makes people indignant. Since I have joined the military, I have made it my goal to maintain peace. The affairs of the country have undergone several changes, but this heart has remained unchanged, and I have vowed to never change it. Moreover, at this critical moment, if anyone is ignorant of the greater good and destroys peace, they should be regarded as a public enemy. I pledge to follow behind you all and proceed in unison to fulfill the original intention of saving the country and the people. As I write this telegram, my thoughts are racing and I cannot express everything I want to say. Please understand. Han Fuju and the commanders of his affiliated divisions and brigades bow in respect." (23rd)

Wang Jun Heads West Yesterday

▲ Solid Defense Around Xuzhou

Xuzhou Express: After Wang Jun was appointed as the Commander-in-Chief of the Third Corps of the Southern Route Group Army, recognizing the need for timely action, he departed Xuzhou this morning (24th) with a contingent of personnel from the Jinpu Garrison Command. The Xuzhou station received notification yesterday and prepared three trains, ready to depart. The first train, a special vehicle for technical troops, and the second train, a military vehicle for the division headquarters, departed successively last night. Wang, due to unfinished business in Xuzhou, only boarded the train at 6:00 AM this morning. Chief of Staff Zhang Jiangui, Secretary Qin Zhenfu, and a contingent of personnel drawn from various departments accompanied Wang. The special train departed at 6:15 AM. The cadre training team lined up at the station, playing music to send them off. Wang said to others that this trip is directly to Xinxiang and that the military action against Shi's army will not pose a significant problem and can be completed in a very short time. The date of return to Xuzhou should not be far off, so the various departments of the garrison command are all left behind in Xuzhou. After Wang's departure to the west, appropriate measures have been taken regarding the issues of the Jinpu Garrison Command and the security of Xuzhou. The duties of the garrison command will be temporarily handled by Chief of General Staff Zhang Jinde. Chief of Staff Qiu Yude will also remain in Xuzhou to assist in all matters. The security of the city is the responsibility of Chen Xueshun, the Director of the Military and Police Supervisory Department. Currently, the defense of Xuzhou is extremely solid. The joint defense conference of the people's militias of the counties along the southern section of the Jinpu Railway, convened by Wang in Xuzhou, is scheduled to be held tomorrow and will be presided over by Chief of General Staff Zhang. A comprehensive plan will be developed for the joint defense of the people's militias of the counties along the railway, from Jiangpu in the south to Lincheng in the north. The defense of the Jinpu Railway is also becoming more solid. As for the Longhai front, the area from Xuzhou to Haizhou has been taken over by Liang Guanying's troops. The area from Xuzhou to Guide has also been taken over by Zhang Lisheng's division, who dispatched cavalry. Therefore, the Longhai route is also extremely secure. (24th)

Recent News on the Suppression of Bandits in Western Anhui's Lu'an

Small Victory on the West Bank of the Pi River

Bengbu Correspondence: The western territory of Lu'an in western Anhui has been occupied by communist bandits for many years. Despite repeated large-scale suppression campaigns by the National Army, it has not been completely cleared due to its proximity to the communist areas on the Henan border. The communist bandits west of the Pi River have become increasingly rampant in recent months, burning, killing, looting, and turning homes into ruins. Refugees are wandering and displaced, with no homes to return to. Those who have fallen into the bandit areas have mostly died. Fortunately, the National Army is holding the east bank of the Pi River, and the eastern territory of Lu'an has been relatively calm. Previously, when the communist bandits invaded eastward, Yuan Jingfu, the head of the Lu'an Communist Eradication Corps, led his troops across the river to meet them in battle, capturing and killing many. County Magistrate Deng rewarded them with 3,000 yuan to show encouragement. Several days ago, the communist bandits west of the river again attempted to invade eastward but were again jointly suppressed by the Communist Eradication Corps and other anti-communist units who crossed the river. They advanced to places such as Zhangjiaji and Guojiadian, capturing six communist bandits alive, killing more than ten, and seizing more than 200 dan of rice, more than 300 dan of paddy, more than 30 pigs, four rifles, and more than 100 primitive guns and cannons. The captured bandits were executed on the spot. One member of the corps was wounded in the battle. The corps is currently holding firm at Zhangkongji, Guojiadian, and other places, preparing to continue the suppression of bandits in places such as Dingjiaji and Huoxingmiao. (22nd)

Rampant Activity of the Great Dao Society in Northern Fujian

▲ Orders Issued to Various Battalions and Teams to Suppress the Society

Fuzhou Correspondence: The counties in northern Fujian are located in the upper reaches of the Min River, with treacherous shoals and steep mountains, making transportation difficult and the people unenlightened. In recent years, bandits have risen in swarms, and people's livelihoods are stretched thin. During the Liu-Lu war in June and July of last year, the Lu's troops were all transferred to the front lines for combat, leaving the rear defenses empty, and the bandit forces became even more rampant, making it impossible for the villagers to live in peace. At this time, a northern monk came to Fujian on a pilgrimage, soliciting donations in various villages between Jian'ou and Nanping. He proclaimed to the masses, "I have come to carry out the will of Heaven, eliminate bandits, and save the people. I have incantations that can defeat bandits and talismans that can ward off bullets." The villagers were deeply fearful of the bandits and did not investigate further, believing him to be true. Many flocked to worship him and convert to his teachings. At one time, there were hundreds of followers. The monk then taught them the art of chanting incantations and drawing talismans, as well as knife techniques. When bandits came, they would gather the masses and attack, first tying blue cloths around their heads, wearing red vests covered with talismans as armor, chanting incantations, and charging forward with knives. The bandits, seeing that they disregarded death and charged desperately, often retreated in defeat. The monk became very proud and proclaimed that his gods were spiritual, and added more embellishments. More and more villagers joined, and they established the Great Dao Society (commonly known as the Great Society), dispatching party members to various villages to set up halls, preach the doctrine, and teach disciples. They also created six precepts: in peacetime, abstain from lust, greed, and doubting the gods; in wartime, abstain from looking sideways, retreating, and letting the enemy escape. Violations would render the spells ineffective and the bullets would penetrate the body. The government, seeing that their actions were superstitious but could assist in resisting bandits, did not stop them. As a result, the society spread extremely rapidly, and within a year, it had spread from Jian'ou and Nanping to Shaxian, Jiangle, Shunchang, Jianyang, Songxi, and Zhenghe, with almost every village having a Great Dao Society hall. They were in constant contact with each other, and their influence became very strong. They also used the slogans of refusing to pay exorbitant taxes and resisting harassment by the army. At that time, the troops stationed in the upper reaches were focusing all their efforts on dealing with the Zhu-Peng communist bandits and had no time to pay attention to them. The party members of the society became even more tyrannical, establishing divine donations, forcing ships and rafts along the river to pay establishment fees, and forcing farmers in the countryside to pay rice by household. Merchants and farmers felt great pain and presented petitions to the provincial and county governments, requesting suppression. The troops stationed in northern Fujian also believed that they were intercepting military weapons and refusing to allow passage, which was a serious disruption to the local area, and were planning to jointly suppress them. They also believed that the monk was the real instigator and issued orders to various battalions and teams, ordering them to find ways to capture him and eradicate the roots. However, the society has considerable power and has spread widely, so it will not be easy to eliminate it. (July 23rd)

Flooding in the Taihu Lake Basin

▲ Rainfall and Water Levels Increase, Nearly Matching 1921 Levels

This year's plum rain season in the Taihu Lake basin has been heavy, and river levels have risen sharply, exceeding the records of the past decade in many places. Since the beginning of the fu period (mid-July to mid-August), there has been continuous rain, and there is a tendency for further increases. A disaster has already formed. According to the latest statistics from the rain and water level measurement reports of the Taihu Lake Basin Water Conservancy Commission of the Ministry of the Interior, since the beginning of [the rainy season], up to the 20th of this month, the rainfall has been the highest in the Yixing, Zhenjiang, Shanghai, and Qingpu areas, reaching 530 to 470 millimeters. The rainfall in Hangzhou, Haiyan, and Jinshan is relatively low. In general, the rainfall in various places has increased by more than double the average of previous flood seasons, nearly matching the total rainfall of August and September of the great flood of 1921. As a result, river levels have risen sharply in recent days. Although they have not reached the levels of the great flood of 1921, the difference is significant. For example, water levels in the Wujin to Yixing area have risen by more than three feet compared to previous years, and the rest have also risen by about one to two feet. Low-lying areas have been widely submerged, resulting in considerable losses. Many villagers have gone to the county government to report crop failures. Stories of dike breaches, collapsed houses, and collapsed city walls are also frequently heard. After the 20th, there have been thunderstorms every day. The heavy rain has continued day and night for the past two days, and the river levels have risen further. The water outside the Xumen gate in Suzhou has reached the shore. Small boats in various places have mostly stopped operating, and navigation is unfavorable. The water in the rivers inside the city has reached the foundations of houses, and low-lying streets have become ditches. Water has entered people's homes, which has not been seen in the past ten years. If the rain continues to fall, the tides will soon arrive, mountain floods will continue, and clear and turbid waters will collide. Inland lakes and marshes will overflow as a result, and the outlets along the river will inevitably be unable to discharge the water, leading to rampant flooding. The great flood disaster of 1921 will reappear today, and the consequences are unimaginable. It is said that the committee is now sending letters to recorders in various places, investigating the flood situation of this year, and ordering them to fill out detailed reports for unified planning.

Suzhou

A Flood Unseen in Ten Years Suzhou has been experiencing continuous heavy rain, and the river water has been rising steadily. The low-lying streets and alleys in the city are ankle-deep in water. The fields and crops in various villages have been submerged, and the price of rice has been rising steadily, jumping by one yuan per stone in two days. At the same time, the river water outside Qimen and Xumen and other places has risen to the shore. There have been dozens of cases of house collapses and injuries inside and outside the city. According to a survey report by the Taihu Lake Water Conservancy Commission, this flood is the worst in ten years, comparable to the great flood of 1911.

Changshu

Zhang Renji's Strange Fire Burned Four More Times Yesterday Zhang Renji's candy store in the north of the city, Zhang Renji, suddenly suffered a fire on the 21st. In half a day, it burned as many as eleven times. Everyone said that it was a fox spirit causing trouble. Now I learned that the store owner, Zhang Jinchang, invited more than a dozen relatives and friends to defend it all night to prevent accidents, and the neighbors also warned each other not to sleep peacefully. There was no movement during the night. It was not until the next morning (23rd) at about 8:00 am that the watchers were very tired and were just drowsily falling asleep. The east corner of the building suddenly became hazy with smoke and fire broke out under the bed. Fortunately, it was spotted immediately and extinguished with water. Afterwards, the fire broke out three more times in two hours. Fortunately, there was someone guarding it, so no major disaster occurred. Later, Zhang Jinchang realized that every time the fire broke out, it was always next to his granddaughter, whether in front or behind her. He had repeatedly seen this without fail. The granddaughter is now thirteen years old, studying at a primary school, and is quite intelligent. The grandfather secretly inquired about the cause of the strange fire. According to the sister, there was nothing different. She had only gone to the Xijin Public Institute in Xilong to play the day before, and a fire broke out when she returned. It is said that the Xijin Public Institute enshrines a fox god, so it may have been brought back, and so on. The shopkeeper was superstitious, in addition to offering a fox seat upstairs, he also sent his granddaughter to live in Shanghai's Qi family temporarily on the 24th.

Continuous Rain and Disaster This place has been experiencing heavy rain since the 5th of this month. The river water has risen sharply, and the fields have been submerged, almost becoming a disaster. Boats to various ports have not yet resumed, and transportation is quite inconvenient. Although there were many sunny days in the middle ten days, the water volume has not receded. On the afternoon of the 22nd, heavy rain suddenly fell again, and by the afternoon of the next day, it was still continuous. The water volume rose more than a foot again. The embankments built by farmers and workers were almost completely washed away by the heavy rain. The fields are still flooded as usual. The rice seedlings have been immersed in water for a long time, and the autumn harvest is hopeless. Now, the district offices have reported the disaster situation to the county government. As for the inland boats to various ports, it was originally planned to resume soon, but after this rainstorm, I am afraid that it will be difficult to recover within ten days.

Wuxi

Continuation of Records on the Wuxi Flood Disaster: The situation of the flood in the county has been detailed in yesterday's report. It is now learned that among the largest embankments in the fifteenth district, only Yangjia Embankment and Laoya'an Embankment can still be salvaged by bailing. Many others cannot be bailed out due to lack of power. Moreover, Yang Qi'an, Shangxia Yang'an, and San Embankments all burst successively the night before, resulting in extremely heavy losses. Fortunately, there are no residents in the embankments, so there have been no losses of people or livestock. In the Beitang area, grain warehouses are all submerged in water and could not be salvaged in time. The wheat in the granaries has gradually sprouted, and there is no way to stack rice. In addition to using pine boards to build high piles, large boats have been rented to temporarily move the grain into the boats. A decision will be made after the water recedes after a long period of sunny weather. However, the losses to both the warehouse and customer sides are extremely large. Yesterday morning, there was a little sunshine, but the sky turned dark in the afternoon, and heavy rain fell again. Traffic between urban and rural areas has slightly recovered. Small boats from Zhangcun, Banqiao, Gushan, Chenshu, Huangtutang, Fangqian, Meicun, Youjiadan, Xueyanqiao, Qianzhou, Laoyaqiao, Hua Dafangzhuang, and other places have all started to sail into the city to facilitate traffic.

Smoke Prohibition After the Abolition of the Investigation Office: Everyone knows the harm of opium. Fortunately, the establishment of the Opium Prohibition Investigation Office was opposed and has been ordered to be abolished. Before the abolition, judicial and administrative organs received clear orders from their superiors that they should not accept cases related to opium administration. Therefore, during this time of transition, it was convenient for opium offenders. Unexpectedly, the Investigation Office, like a flash in the pan, still wants to strictly prohibit opium. However, the judicial organs have not yet received a clear order to accept cases as usual, so there have been instances of refusal to accept cases. A few days ago, the Ninth Branch of the County Public Security Bureau arrested several red pill offenders in the countryside and submitted them to the County Public Security Bureau, which transferred them to the County Court for interrogation. At that time, the court had not yet received a clear order to accept cases, so there was once a refusal. After receiving the clear order, they accepted cases as usual. However, the public security branches have stopped carrying out arrests for several days.

Robbers Repeatedly Robbed and Injured People in Kaihua Township: Since Chen Chuande took office as the county magistrate of this county, there has been no day without robbery cases in the four townships. The prospect of public security is precarious. In Nian Qi-San Tu (273 Tu), Jinxi Bridge area of the fourteenth district (Kaihua Township), resident Zhu Yude, who runs an iron shop on Baixianqiao in Shanghai, is considered well-off. At 12 o'clock in the evening the other day, amid heavy rain, the village dogs barked wildly. Zhu's wife, Song, and his son, Agou, heard the sound and suspected that thieves had come. They immediately put on their clothes and got out of bed to open the door and look out. Suddenly, seven or eight robbers wearing black short jackets, speaking a mixture of local and Hakka dialects, appeared. Several of the robbers were only in their twenties, each holding a handgun and candles. Three robbers stood guard outside the door, while the remaining robbers entered the house to search and rob, and tied up Song and her son, as well as their adopted daughter-in-law, demanding to know where the money was hidden. As a result, more than one hundred yuan in cash was robbed. After the robbers obtained the loot, they were not satisfied and broke the walls in Zhu's house. They also forced their way into the home of the widow Lu Dong, tied her hands behind her back, and burned her left breast and left wrist with candles. Lu Dong had no choice but to offer five yuan in banknotes to the robbers. Seeing this, the robbers thought that Lu Dong was cunning and took out a handgun and shot at the ground to intimidate her. Unexpectedly, the bullet hit her right instep, and blood flowed like a river. She fell to the ground in extreme pain. Seeing that they had injured someone, the robbers shouted and fled. After checking, the loss was several dozen yuan. Yesterday, her sister-in-law, Xu, sent the injured person to the city by boat and admitted her to the Brothers Hospital for treatment.

Petition from the Inn Industry: The inn industry in Wujin County petitioned because the Public Security Bureau decided to have the police from the branch offices and outposts conduct overnight inspections of inns to eliminate opium, gambling, and prostitution, which has a great impact on the business of inns. Therefore, at 10 a.m. on the 25th, they sent representatives Pang Baosheng and five others to the County Chamber of Commerce to petition. Lin Junbao received them and, after discussing the results, Mr. Lin agreed to contact the Public Security Bureau and then determine a solution. The six representatives then went to the Public Security Bureau to petition. The chief of the First Section, Wang Xiaowu, received them. After a long discussion, Chief Wang consulted with Mr. Lin of the Chamber of Commerce by telephone. As a result, it was temporarily decided that each inn would be routinely inspected from 9 p.m. to 12 a.m. by the responsible branch office and outpost. Special inspections would be conducted by the Public Security Bureau from 1 a.m. to 3 a.m. The representatives then took their leave.

Resolution of Automobile Donation in Various Counties North of the Yangtze River: The Construction Department previously convened the heads of the Construction Bureaus of various counties north of the Yangtze River to discuss the implementation of collecting automobile donations according to the new regulations. All car owners unanimously went on strike against the donation. Yangzhou

Joint Meeting of Principals Opposing the New Budget: The principals of various primary schools in Jiangdu County believe that there are many inappropriate aspects of the new education budget compiled by the administrative side. Therefore, they held a meeting yesterday to discuss the reasons, which are as follows: (1) The budget for the 20th year was not approved by the Education Administration Conference, but was compiled solely by the bureau chief, which is considered inappropriate. (2) The teaching time per grade in primary school is approximately 1,200 minutes or more. The new standard requires one person, which is impossible for one person to handle and complete since people are not omnipotent; those who can teach Chinese and arithmetic may not be able to teach music, physical education, art, and crafts; those who can teach music, physical education, art, and crafts may not be able to teach Chinese and arithmetic. (3) The education administration and social education agencies have not been reduced, but primary school education alone has been reduced again and again, which is considered unfair. (4) The previous National Assembly had a resolution to improve the treatment of primary school education, and the Ministry of Education also had a clear order to improve the treatment of primary school teachers. Now, Director Chen is compiling the budget for the 20th year, reducing primary school funding, which is a violation of orders. (5) The Jiangdu education financial situation is difficult, not because of the large expenditure, but because the income cannot be organized. The collectors of the right book and school land miscellaneous donations are heavily in arrears. The bureau chief is not good at urging and organizing collections, but only reduces expenses, which is unreasonable. Based on the above five points, the following two resolutions were made: (1) Request the Education Association to actively appeal to the provincial, county, and bureau authorities. (2) Send representatives to Zhenjiang with the standing committee members of the Education Association to petition. Yang Chuqing and Jin Shengfu were immediately decided as the representatives.

Heavy Rain Again Yesterday for a Day and Night: In the area north of the Yangtze River, there has been the most rain in the past half month. The Yangtze River tide and lake water are already showing signs of an unmanageable disaster. Unexpectedly, heavy rain poured down again in Yangzhou City from the evening of the 23rd until 9 p.m. on the 24th, causing the ground water to rise by more than a foot. On that day, not only were ships and automobiles not operating, but long-distance telephone lines were also unable to connect due to the rain. The Shanghai newspapers have not arrived for three days. Eight or nine out of ten poor people are running out of food. The phenomenon of widespread suffering is being realized in the city. The severity of the disaster can be seen from this. Zhang Zhijiang, the Jiangsu Pacification Commissioner, convened a meeting of the main personnel of various agencies due to the continuous heavy rain and frequent reports of disasters in various places. Taking Yangzhou City as an example, most of the streets and alleys have become swamps. He convened an emergency meeting last night (the 24th) to discuss prevention and emergency relief methods. The attendees included Chen Changwei, a member of the County Party Department, the brigade commander of the 94th Brigade, Chen, the county magistrate of the County Government, Wang, the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, An, the director of the Public Security Bureau, Feng, the director of the Construction Bureau, and Shao, the director of the Jiangdu Section of the Engineering Office. Yu Dianshu, the chief of staff of the Commissioner's Office, presided over the meeting and discussed prevention measures: (1) When the water in the Grand Canal along the border of Jiangdu rises to the shore, sandbags can be used for prevention. (2) Pay attention to preventing the westward water from flowing eastward. (3) The municipal and county governments and the Construction Bureau will jointly provide relief to the residents in the city who have been flooded. (4) Quickly seek emergency relief methods for the disaster areas in the four townships.

Danyang

Robbery and Injury in Yuanjia Village: Farmers Tao Tianjue's house in Yuanjia Village, East Township, was suddenly attacked by many bandits the other night, each armed with guns and weapons. They broke into the house and shouted to silence the residents. They looted and searched violently. The Tao family members did not have time to escape and were imprisoned in one room. The bandits demanded the surrender of silver dollars, but their demands were not met. They tied up the housewife, stabbed her right arm with a knife, and shot through the owner's right leg. After about an hour, they escaped with their loot.

Change of Prison Officer: Li Yurui, the prison officer of this county, has now been transferred to Songjiang by order of the High Court. His vacancy will be filled by Zheng Ligeng.

Jiaxing

Opening of the Vagrant Vocational Training Center: The Jiaxing County Qingxiang Bureau, during this period of handling Qingxiang matters, sent a letter to the county government to plan the establishment of a vagrant vocational training center. The county government has planned funds and organized its establishment. On one hand, the vagrants detained by the Qingxiang Bureau have been sent to the vocational training center for custody. It is now known that a continuous stream of vagrants, already numbering thirty-seven, has been sent. The internal workshops have also been prepared and will officially start work on the 26th. They are divided into four departments: cotton weaving, sewing, printing, and sock weaving.

Continuous Rain Brings Disaster, Fields and Crops Submerged: Jiaxing has been experiencing continuous rain, and the river water has risen sharply. The northern countryside has become a swamp. The fields are indistinguishable, and the rice crops are completely submerged. Although the farmers have tried to protect them, the rain has not stopped, so there is no effect. They have reported the disaster to the county government. The County Agricultural Association has convened an emergency meeting to request funds for water conservancy in western Zhejiang to urgently repair the dikes. At the same time, it has sent letters to the village councils in various rural areas to urge farmers to repair the embankment dikes, and has submitted a request to the county government to strictly prohibit the passage of steamships. The small steamships operating to various ports have all suspended operations for many days due to the rising water.

Hangzhou

Impact of Heavy Rain on Hangzhou-Changxing and Hangzhou-Pingyao Roads: Due to the continuous heavy rain and mountain floods, the road surface of the Hangzhou-Changxing Highway from Jingshan to Shijiaqiao has been washed away for three or four zhang. Therefore, the route was temporarily suspended from the 23rd. The Provincial Highway Bureau sent personnel to repair it, and it resumed operation on the afternoon of the 24th. Unexpectedly, there was heavy rain all night on the 25th, which did not stop until noon yesterday (the 26th). The water level in the Pingyao to Penggongling area of the road rose by two or three feet, and the route was suspended again in the afternoon. At 3 p.m., the water receded gradually, and tickets were sold as usual. After the heavy rain on the Hangzhou-Pingyao Road, the mud and rocks on the road surface from Qibao to Qiaosi were loose and cracked, and vehicles could not travel. The director of the Highway Administration Bureau, Huang, immediately ordered the chief of the engineering section, Sun Faduan, to supervise the workers to rush to repair the road overnight. Due to the importance of traffic, the route is scheduled to operate as usual today (the 27th) to facilitate travel. It is also heard that a small chartered car from Moganshan to Hangzhou was driven to Penggongling during the flood. Because the water was quite high, the interior was also wet. After stopping to repair the engine, a large fish about a foot long jumped into the car and was carried to Hangzhou, which is also an interesting story.

Tragedy of a Child Falling into a Pot and Being Boiled to Death: A Jiangbei barge named Cao, in Gongbu Dakou, was boiling water in the cabin after unloading goods yesterday morning. His wife and child were lying on the cabin floor. The child was three years old and had not yet been weaned. Unexpectedly, Cao's wife fell asleep due to fatigue. Cao was also talking with friends on the shore. The child accidentally turned over and fell into the pot. The water was boiling, and the child was boiled to death. Cao's wife woke up in surprise, but it was too late to save him.

Ningbo

Homeowners Strongly Oppose the Construction of an Airport: The site of the Wangjiawan Airport outside the West Gate of this port has been completely surveyed yesterday, totaling about 500 mu, with about 300 graves. The farmers and villagers in the bay believe that after the airport is built, the fields will be requisitioned and the houses will have to be demolished. Therefore, at noon yesterday, more than 200 men, women, old and young people gathered at the office of the neighborhood committee to make noise, demanding that the county government strive to prevent the construction of the airport. The neighborhood chief had no idea what to do, so he telephoned the Yin County government. After receiving the call, County Magistrate Chen sent two section members, Zhang Leyao and Chen Bangji, to explain, saying that the construction of the airport was ordered by the General Headquarters and had to be completed within a month. Although the county government knew the various losses of the residents, it was limited by official regulations and was truly in a difficult situation. Since the facts are as they are, it is best to elect a few representatives to express their opinions so that they can be conveyed and adopted. Later, the farmers elected Wang Xiazi and three others to express three opinions: (1) The early rice must be harvested before construction can begin. (2) The county government must assess and compensate for the losses of the farmers. (3) The county government must find a way to take care of the families who make a living by renting fields. Zhang and Chen promised to convey these opinions, and the villagers dispersed.

Tian Shulan, Who is Traveling Around the Country, Arrives in Ningbo: Tian Shulan from Hunan, who is determined to travel around the country, set off from Hangzhou on the 23rd and arrived in Ningbo. The planned travel period is six years. He will start from Shanghai, return to Shanghai, and then make the great move to travel around the world.

Shaoxing

Negotiations Completed for the 200,000 Yuan Provincial Loan: The case of the Zhejiang Finance Department borrowing 200,000 yuan from the silver and money industries in Shaoxing has now been successfully negotiated. It has been designated that the new and old land tax silver and rice taxes in Shaoxing County will be collected and repaid as soon as possible. All previous unpaid unified donation loans of 150,000 yuan will be converted into new and old land tax repayments, with a monthly interest rate of one cent. Taxes will be collected daily, and the bureau will hand them over to the county treasury for special storage. In addition to paying the interest of more than 13,000 yuan under the previous unified donation loan, the funds will be allocated and paid in full from the previous special funds. The county bureau's monthly administrative expenses, as well as the food rations for the inmates in the prison and detention center, will still be allocated from the collected regular tax. When the remaining funds accumulate to 10,000 yuan, the loan will be repaid once, with interest reduced accordingly until it is fully repaid. This method has now been approved by the Finance Department, ordering the county bureau to sign a loan agreement with the representatives of the silver and money industries on a specific date.

Thorough Investigation of Tang Renping's Rice Losses: The case of Tang Rixin, the former county magistrate of Shaoxing, failing to handle rice price stabilization and causing huge losses is being thoroughly investigated by Weng Shuiping, who was sent by the Department of Civil Affairs to Shaoxing yesterday. Because this case involves the waste of local public funds, Commissioner Weng convened a meeting of local public organizations unrelated to the Food Maintenance Association at the county government on the morning of the 26th to discuss responsibility and the disposal of stored rice.

Qu County

Trial Operation of Traffic on the Quzhou-Changshan Road: The automobile route from Changshan in western Zhejiang to Yushan in eastern Jiangxi has long been opened to traffic. However, the automobile road from Qu County to Changshan, which has been contracted by the Hengchang Long-Distance Automobile Company for a long time, was originally scheduled to open to traffic this year. Due to the importance of suppressing bandits in eastern Jiangxi and the need for military transportation on the road, the company spared no expense to hire thousands of workers to rush to build the road day and night. It has now been completed. At 8 a.m. on the 21st of this month, the company borrowed two automobiles from the Changyu Automobile Company and carried passengers from Changshan to Qu County. The Wanchuan Engineering Office also sent empty cars to Shuanggangkou to welcome Wu Bokang, the county magistrate of Qu County, Lu Zutao, the chief of the Construction Section, and Xiang Hualing and Chen Mu, the company's preparatory committee members, to the Wanchuan Engineering Office for a meal and took a photo before dispersing.

Anqing

Change of County Magistrates in Fuyang, Chaoxian, and Hefei: The Provincial Government's Standing Committee approved the change of county magistrates in three counties on the 25th. Wang Yunlong, the county magistrate of Fuyang County, was dismissed from his post and investigated. His vacancy will be filled by Liu Fohang, the county magistrate of Chaoxian County. The vacancy left by him will be filled by Zhang Shusen, the county magistrate of Hefei County. The vacant position of county magistrate of Hefei County will be provisionally filled by Zhou Junnan.

Provincial Government Allocates Funds to Aid Relief in Jiangxi Disaster: The Provincial Government's Standing Committee on the 24th, due to receiving a cold telegram from Xiong Shiyao and others in Nanchang, stated that the Red Disaster in Jiangxi Province was spreading and ravaging more than 50 counties, with more than 4 million people fleeing. An order was issued to establish a relief agency to plan relief matters. It was dared to launch an emergency relief effort, and it was decided to order the Finance Department to allocate 2,000 yuan in relief funds to be remitted immediately.

Local News

Jinghu Railway Expected to Fully Reopen Today

▲Traffic Between Nanjing and Zhenjiang Resumed Yesterday

The Jinghu Railway has been unable to fully operate for two days since it was blocked due to heavy rain. Upbound trains only ran to Zhenjiang Nanmen Station, and downbound trains also started from there. An investigation with the Railway Bureau yesterday revealed that traffic between Nanjing and Zhenjiang had resumed at 10 a.m. yesterday. The mudslide from Baogai Mountain on the section from Zhenjiang Station to Zhenjiang Nanmen Station has been removed by three-quarters. It is expected that it will be completely removed after 7 or 8 p.m. yesterday. After the roadbed is repaired, the entire line is expected to be open to traffic around 4 or 5 a.m. today. The various news obtained yesterday is recorded below:

▲Nanjing-Zhenjiang Trains Restored: According to the Traffic Department of the Railway Bureau, the roadbed between Nanjing and Zhenjiang has been repaired and resumed normal traffic at 10 a.m. yesterday. However, passengers who need to pass through Nanjing can get off at Zhenjiang Nanmen Station, walk along the road next to the station to Zhenjiang Station, and then buy tickets to change trains to Beijing. Only the section from Zhenjiang Station to Zhenjiang Nanmen Station on the entire Jinghu line is still under repair.

▲Entire Line May Reopen This Morning: According to the engineer's report to the Traffic Department, the section of track from Zhenjiang Station to Zhenjiang Nanmen Station must be repaired after 6 p.m. on the 26th. After removing the mudslide from Baogai Mountain, the roadbed can be repaired, and traffic can be restored this morning. The upbound night express train that departed from the North Station at 11:45 p.m. yesterday has been ordered by the Traffic Department to arrive at Zhenjiang Nanmen Station at 5:36 a.m. this morning. If the track has been repaired there, it can be driven directly to Nanjing and then back to Shanghai. Therefore, there is a possibility that the entire Jinghu line will resume full operation from 5:45 a.m. this morning.

Jinpu Railway Also Blocked by Rain Yesterday

▲Joint Transport Tickets Temporarily Suspended

The section between Huaqiying and Dongge stations on the Jinpu Railway was also blocked by the deep water and damage to the tracks caused by the flooding yesterday morning. All trains were temporarily suspended, and the Beijing-Pingyao-Liaotong trains were also suspended. All routes were notified to temporarily suspend the sale of joint transport tickets. Efforts are currently being made to divert the water to facilitate repairs. It is estimated that normal traffic will be restored in two or three days.

Anti-Japanese Association Decides on Methods for Storing Japanese Goods

▲ Confiscations in Zhabei, Pudong, and Nanshi

▲ All Departments to Work as Usual on Sundays

▲ Customs Brokers to Refuse Handling of Japanese Goods Starting Today

After commencing inspection work, the Anti-Japanese and Aid-the-Overseas-Chinese Committee has confiscated Japanese goods at its three inspection branches in Nanshi, Zhabei, and Pudong. The committee held its third executive meeting yesterday to discuss methods for managing confiscated Japanese goods, taking an extremely cautious approach. Details of the reports are as follows:

▲ Confiscated Japanese Goods: According to official reports from the committee's inspection department, the quantity of Japanese goods confiscated in recent days is as follows: (1) On the 23rd, the Zhabei inspection station confiscated eleven cases of foreign cloth and flannel of brands such as Shen Tai Transport Company's "Fu Lu Jin Ji" and Gong Yi Company's "Zhi Gong Ni" two cases, also Qing Ji Company six pieces of printed cloth and three bales of foreign cloth at the North Railway Station. (2) On the 24th, the Pudong inspection station confiscated two civilian boats hired by Lu Yang Gong near the Lu Jia Du Ningxing wharf, containing 132 pieces of foreign cloth and 130 pieces of Wanxing Company's foreign yarn, and 20 pieces of Ri Xin Foreign Firm's "Magpie" brand foreign yarn, all temporarily stored in the Gongda warehouse at Lu Jia Du. (3) On the 24th, the Zhabei inspection station confiscated 106 pieces of foreign cloth, flannel, etc., belonging to Qing Ji Company at the Maigen Road station, and also 30 bales of Weida Silk Factory's rayon, three large bales of double thread, and 13 pieces of Zhi Gong Ni foreign yarn, etc., on Baoshan Road. (4) From the 23rd to the 24th, the Nanshi inspection station confiscated a total of 493 pieces of Japanese goods, all numbered and counted for storage in the warehouse, with the Transportation Industry Association providing responsible documentation for verification.

▲ Storage Methods: The methods for storing confiscated Japanese goods were seriously discussed at yesterday's third executive meeting. At the same time, based on the proposal of Chen Songyuan, convener of the Design Committee, it was advocated that several designated public warehouses be used. Whenever goods are confiscated, in addition to counting the number of items on the spot, issuing a receipt, and handing it over to the owner, the goods should be immediately sent to the public warehouse for storage. After detailed research, the following storage methods were decided: (1) Confiscated goods should be sent to the warehouse at any time. (2) Immediately after confiscation, the inspection department should notify the investigation department to investigate whether the goods are indeed Japanese goods. (3) After storage, the warehouse receipt should be sent to the storage department for inspection and safekeeping. (4) When confiscating goods, the quantity of items recorded on the goods should not only be based on the number of items in order to prevent abuses. (5) After confiscation, the inspection department should issue a receipt to the owner of the goods. (6) Confiscated goods should be published daily in the newspaper's news column for easy reference. (7) The release of goods must be decided by the executive committee. (8) Confiscation and release of goods should be reported to the executive committee.

▲ Return of British Goods: On the 24th, the Zhabei inspection station of the inspection department confiscated 30 bales of rayon and three large bales of double thread belonging to the Weida Silk Factory on Baoshan Road. Subsequently, the factory came to the committee and claimed that the goods were British goods and brought the order as proof. The committee's investigation department went to investigate and confirmed that the 30 bales of rayon were indeed British goods, while the three large bales of double thread were determined to be Japanese goods. The report was submitted to the executive committee, and the executive committee decided that the rayon should be returned, and the double thread should be retained and await disposal.

▲ Executive Meeting: The committee held its third executive meeting at 2 p.m. the day before yesterday. Executive committee members Wang Xiaolai, Chen Tingrui, Wang Yansong, Lu Jingtu, Tao Baichuan, and Hou Dachun were present. Lu Jingtu was elected as chairman. The following resolutions were passed: (1) The heads of each department should be fully responsible for the staff in their respective departments. (2) In addition to the regular meeting time from 11 a.m. to 1 p.m. daily, it was also stipulated that daily executive committee members should be on duty: Hou Dachun on Mondays, Wu Xiaolai on Tuesdays, Tao Baichuan on Wednesdays, Yu Qiaqing on Thursdays, Wang Yansong on Fridays, Chen Tingrui on Saturdays, and Lu Jingshi on Sundays. (3) The office hours of each department were set from 9 a.m. to 6 p.m. (4) Executive committee members Tao Baichuan and Lu Jingshi were appointed to review the two sets of regulations on awards and punishments. (5) Executive committee member Wang Yansong proposed to form a storage committee to ensure caution and also resigned from the position of director of the storage department. It was decided to form a storage committee and submit it to the executive committee for discussion. The resignation should be rejected with words of comfort. (6) The inspection department's report was discussed regarding how to dispose of old Japanese bottles found at the South Railway Station. It was decided to temporarily detain them. (7) It was decided whether Japanese raw materials and necessities could be allowed to pass through. It was decided that movement should be stopped during the registration period, but in special circumstances, the committee should be registered first, and after the committee's investigation and verification, a temporary pass certificate would be issued. (8) It was decided to nominate candidates for secretary. It was decided to nominate Committee Member Yan Esheng to concurrently serve as chief secretary and Committee Member Feng Yixian to concurrently serve as secretary, and submit it to the executive committee.

▲ Sunday Office Hours: The committee decided to work as usual on Sundays due to the tense anti-Japanese work, with the same hours as usual, from 9 a.m. to 6 p.m. Therefore, all departments were still very busy yesterday.

▲ Implementation of Refusal to Load: The Transportation and Customs Broker Association convened a general meeting of members at 3 p.m. yesterday to discuss measures for economic severance with Japan. Over 400 representatives from China Merchants Yu Ye attended. Chairman Shi Zhikun reported the contents of the letter from the Anti-Japanese and Aid-the-Overseas-Chinese Committee, and then began discussions. It was decided to implement the automatic refusal to load Japanese goods starting tomorrow (the 27th).

▲ Joint Association Telegram: The Shanghai Machine-Made National Goods Factory United Association sent a telegram stating: To all newspapers, all levels of party headquarters, all institutions, and all organizations nationwide, Recently, Japanese police in Wanbaoshan shot and killed our country's farmers and instigated Korean people to riot and brutally massacre overseas Chinese in Korea. Shocking telegrams have been sent, and we are deeply indignant. Such brutal behavior is intolerable to the world and not permitted by public law. Who has no parents, who has no siblings, who has no spouse, who has no relatives and friends? Reading investigation reports and communications from all parties, the cries of sorrow and pain are inhumane and shocking. Such brutal behavior, if not instigated by someone, would not be so bold and reckless. The members of this association, after painful reflection, emulate the meaning of letting down hair and tying crowns, believing that the Japanese government should be fully responsible for this type of case. In addition to waiting for our national government to deal with the matter seriously, our self-help method is to adopt a self-sufficient policy, strive to produce, and control its source, without overt forms of resistance, to achieve the effect of developing industry. When it comes to saving the country, there is nothing better than this. This association, as a group of national goods factories, has taken promoting the national goods industry as its duty. Outwardly, we fear the neighboring country's atrocities; inwardly, we worry about the decline of popular morale. We dare to make an urgent appeal to make a slight contribution. We deeply hope that those in power in the government will remember the national crisis, support each other, reduce donations and taxes, and eliminate corruption. We also hope that our comrades in the national goods industry at home and abroad will rise up together, complete this ambition, and strive to produce, which is to save ourselves, and also to save the country and save people. We offer these tearful words, hoping for your consideration. Shanghai Machine-Made National Goods Factory United Association.

▲ Minhang Rises Up: After the Shanghai County First District Minhang All Circles Anti-Japanese and Aid-the-Overseas-Chinese Committee member candidates were approved by the local party headquarters, the first committee meeting was held yesterday. Committee members Zhang Boliang, Zhou Meisun, Tao Shaochun, Yu Zhenchi, and others, fourteen in total, attended. Zhang Jingling, representative of the Chamber of Commerce, presided, and Peng Yu recorded. The key matters were decided: (1) Zhang Jingling, Chen Lujun, Shen Jingzhi, Peng Yu, and Wu Shifang were elected as standing committee members of this committee, and Zhang Jingling was elected as chairman and Peng Yu as secretary. (2) Zhang Boliang, Li Hengzhai, Jin Zuobin, Tao Shaochun, Wu Jingqing, Liu Yunshu, and Ding Zixiang were elected as supervisors of this committee. (3) Peng Yu, Dong Jingliang, and Shen Jingzhi were asked to draft the organization's outline of this committee to be passed at the next meeting. (4) The National Government was requested to negotiate seriously with the Japanese side and provide assistance to the overseas Chinese with real strength. (5) The general outline for boycotting Japanese goods was decided: (A) Notify all businesses to return the goods that have been ordered as soon as possible, and stop shipping the goods that have been ordered but have not yet arrived at the port. Japanese goods that have been purchased must be registered with the committee within a time limit. (B) Omitted. (6) This committee is divided into five sections: General Affairs, Publicity, Registration, Inspection, and Storage. (7) Shen Jing was appointed as the director of the General Affairs Section, Zhu Jiasheng as the director of the Publicity Section, Dai Zuping as the director of the Inspection Section, Chen Jifang as the director of the Registration Section, and Zhang Boliang as the director of the Storage Section. (8) It was determined that the committee would meet once every two weeks, and the standing committee would meet once a week. (9) A "Minhang All Circles Anti-Japanese and Aid-the-Overseas-Chinese Committee Seal" was made. (10) This committee will start work immediately. (11) The Minhang Chamber of Commerce is temporarily used as the address of the committee. (12) Zhang Jingling, Shen Jing, and Wu Shifang were appointed to attend the county's Anti-Japanese and Aid-the-Overseas-Chinese Conference. The meeting adjourned.

Shanghai-Xiamen Radio is Operating Smoothly as Usual

The short-wave radio station from the Ministry of Communications in Shanghai to Xiamen has been operating exceptionally well in recent days, resulting in the original generator being insufficient. Currently, Shanghai and Xiamen each have three generators for communication. Chinese Eggs Will Be Severely Hit After the Success of the Soviet Russian Plan

▲ Hope the Government Has a Way to Take Care of the Aftermath

Our country's egg exports have gradually become one of the main exports since the European War. Recently, due to the high price of gold and the low price of silver, there should be good results, but the result is the opposite. Because the world's production is excessive, prices are low, and egg prices have fallen sharply. Our country's egg merchants have suffered losses and are all disappointed. Moreover, the United States has repeatedly increased import egg taxes, and Japan is striving to supply itself. The Pacific route is gradually becoming extinct. The only thing that can decorate the foreign market is Europe. In the Soviet Russian government's five-year plan, the egg production industry is also striving for rapid progress, trying to regain the position of leader in the world's egg industry before the European War. 64 million gold was allocated specifically for expanding the egg industry. In addition to cultivating egg chickens to increase production, the plan also includes building five large-scale egg factories, and increasing the number of new-style egg warehouses to 567, new-style chicken coops to 377, and building 79 new cold storage warehouses. It is estimated that after the completion of the above plan, 1.36 trillion eggs can be produced annually. In addition to supplying domestic consumption of about 1 trillion, there will be a surplus of 360 billion eggs that can be sold abroad (approximately 2.2 million long boxes). It is estimated that this year's egg exports from our country will be about 90,000 to 100,000 long boxes, only slightly less than one-twenty-second of the surplus from the Soviet Union. In the future, Russian eggs will be devalued and dumped, which will severely hit Chinese eggs. In addition, after our country increased the huge export egg tax, egg merchants have been affected. Recently, Anhui Province has also had an egg industry business tax incident, which was contracted by a few people, and business tax was levied on egg farms, ignoring the instructions of the Ministry of Finance (the Ministry of Finance approved and ordered the Anhui Finance Department to exempt business tax for those who only buy and do not sell to the customers). This is truly the misfortune of the egg industry. We hope that those in power will take care of the aftermath.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Asks for Relief for the Flour Industry

▲ Levy Import Tax on Foreign Flour

▲ And Reduce the Uniform Tax on Chinese Flour

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry to provide relief to my country's flour industry. The original text said: The request was submitted, and on the 23rd of this month, the flour factory industry association of this city and the Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui inland machine-made flour factory association jointly stated in a letter that since the Qing Jiawu period, wheat began to be subject to a production and sales tax of four cents of silver per stone, while flour was generally exempted from tax throughout the country. Until July 17 of the Republic of China, an order from the Ministry of Finance was issued, exempting wheat from tax and instead levying a special tax on wheat flour of one jiao per bag of foreign currency. Examining the practices of various countries in the world, wheat flour is generally not taxed, but the import tax on foreign flour is very heavy. When the regulations on the special tax on wheat flour were promulgated, it was the beginning of construction after the success of the Northern Expedition. The merchants and people expressed their obedience, originally hoping that after unification, the government would automatically abolish it to meet the world's trend and comfort the merchants and people's expectations. However, since the tax was levied, it has been three years. The flour merchants have fulfilled their obligations, which cannot be said to be not many, but there is still no import tax on foreign flour, allowing it to be imported as much as possible and dumping it. China's flour industry is still in its infancy, and how can it resist? Moreover, the special tax on wheat flour was originally to offset the wheat tax. Now, under the business tax food item, wheat has not been excluded. Although the nature and name of the tax are different, in reality, it has restored the previous wheat tax situation. Examining the business tax on food, only 2 or 3 per mille is levied. For example, wheat flour is subject to a uniform tax of one jiao per bag, which is 3%. How far apart is it? Moreover, flour shops must pay business tax before they are allowed to sell flour. Wheat is taxed, wheat flour is taxed when it leaves the factory, and it is taxed again when it is sold. Three taxes on one item, how can merchants and people bear it? The current value of gold is soaring, and the prices of all metals and materials are rising. The cost of flour factories has increased, and the selling price cannot be resisted due to the dumping of foreign flour. In addition, with the 3% uniform tax, manufacturers are struggling to make ends meet. The country had no choice but to levy taxes on the people's food. We should ask your association to submit to the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, and the Ministry of Industry for review and approval to reduce the uniform tax rate on wheat flour to show generosity, which will benefit both commerce and people's livelihood. On the one hand, for the import of foreign flour, we should follow the precedents of various countries and heavily levy import taxes to stop loopholes. This matter is related to the vital interests of the flour industry, and we sincerely appeal and are extremely eager to wait for orders, etc., to be sent to the meeting. Upon inquiry, this matter was first received by the Tianjin General Chamber of Commerce in January of this year, stating that Tianjin flour factories were affected by the dumping of foreign flour. Of the original eight factories, only one remains, and it is necessary to provide assistance. We should submit to the Department for a reward fund method, for the Chinese factory's uniform tax, a certain percentage should be refunded, or for the low-priced dumping of foreign flour, the current anti-dumping tax law should be applied, and an anti-dumping tax should be levied. Afterwards, the Department issued Order No. 5214, stating that according to the association's previous transfer of the decline of Tianjin flour industry, please prepare a foreign flour consumption tax to maintain domestic goods, etc., the situation was reported to the Ministry of Finance for review and handling, and a telegram was sent on its behalf. This has been approved. The case was previously transferred by the Hebei Finance Commissioner. At that time, the situation was instructed to be observed, and a plan was prepared and reported. It is known that the previous reasons should be checked and notified, etc. This was approved. A notice was issued to the association, etc. It has been a long time since then. How exactly the plan was prepared and reported has not been informed. The Tianjin Chamber of Commerce claimed that foreign flour used to be sold to our country's interior, and taxes had to be paid everywhere, approximately one jiao and six or seven fen per bag. In addition, the two flour factory associations stated that wheat used to be subject to a production and sales tax of only four cents of silver per stone, while flour was generally exempted from tax throughout the country. Afterwards, special taxes and uniform taxes were implemented in turn, with Chinese and foreign flour being subject to the same tax rate. According to the above situation, although Chinese flour raw materials have been granted the grace of tax exemption, in practice, it is just changing the tax to a tax, which is equal to nothing. However, foreign flour, due to the uniform tax, has been reduced and is more popular. All of this refers to the time before the business tax was handled. Since the business tax was levied on wheat, considering the situation, although it is not a tax on objects, it is the common practice of businessmen to seek profit. The amount of tax they bear will inevitably be added to the price of wheat. Chinese factories have the concern that the price of raw materials will increase, while foreign flour is imported from foreign countries, and the raw materials are not affected by the price increase, so it can be sold cheaply. The difficulties listed by the two associations can supplement the previous letter from the Tianjin General Chamber of Commerce. According to the letter's content, we should prepare a document to submit to the Ministry for review and approval, and handle it separately as requested by the association to maintain industry, which is in the public interest.

Seaport Quarantine Office Temporarily Suspends Disinfection of Sailing Ships

▲ Boat Gangs' Opposing Attitude is Firm

▲ Quarantine Office Reports to the General Office for Handling

The Wusong Seaport Quarantine Office, following the order of Wu Liande, Director of the National Seaport Quarantine Office, strictly prevents plague and has formulated five disinfection rules for ships. Starting this month, imported large and small sand fishing boats from the north and south gangs will also be disinfected with medicinal water. Unexpectedly, the merchant boat gangs at Songkou believe that the disinfection procedures are complicated and time-consuming, and they feel that the disinfection fee charged by the office is too high and cannot be borne, so they have united and firmly opposed it. In recent days, all imported large and small ships have refused to allow medical officers to board the ship to carry out disinfection procedures. The Chinese and Western medical officers of the office, seeing this situation, were deeply afraid of accidents, so they temporarily suspended the disinfection of sailing ships from the day before yesterday. According to Chinese officials of the office yesterday, epidemic prevention work is important, and sailing ship disinfection is necessary and will not be terminated due to the opposition of the boat merchants. Moreover, foreign small barges have all been disinfected in accordance with the regulations, which is an international practice, so there is no objection. If domestic sailing ships are not disinfected, foreigners will criticize it. The office has reported to Director Wu of the National Seaport Quarantine Office for instructions. The sailing ship disinfection fee was originally set at ten taels and five taels. It is true that the poor boat households of the second-class sailing ships cannot afford it. Perhaps it will be reduced to five taels and two and a half taels to alleviate the difficulties of the merchants. This issue must also be resolved after Director Wu arrives in Shanghai today (yesterday).

Municipal Health Bureau Urges Registration of Hospitals in the City

The Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau conducts annual registration of public and private hospitals established in the Chinese Concession. According to Article 17 of the Hospital Management Regulations, each hospital must submit a report on its treatment overview for the year in two phases: before July 15th for the first phase and before January 15th of the following year for the second phase, filling out the prescribed forms and submitting them to the health authority. However, the registration for the first phase of this year has already passed, and many hospitals have delayed reporting. The bureau has specifically instructed all public and private hospitals in the city to report to the bureau for registration according to the prescribed format for evaluation.

Jisheng Society Receives Disaster Reports from Various Provinces

The Chinese Jisheng Society has recently received successive reports from various groups in Anhui Province, including Huaining, Fengyang, Linhua Town, Fengtai, Fuyang, Huaiyuan, Wuhe, Quanjiao, and Suxian counties, and Jiangxi Province, including Xinjian County and Fuyou, stating that in addition to bandit disasters, continuous rain for weeks has caused devastating floods, the worst in decades. People's livelihoods are in dire straits, and they have no time to escape. Rice and autumn grain have been completely submerged, and livestock, people, houses, utensils, food, clothing, and property have been lost by tens or hundreds of millions. The number of deaths is countless. The affected areas inside and outside the city and villages are specifically reported and are too numerous to list. In Henan Province, Guangshan, Luoshan, Gushi, Shangcheng, Dengxian, Nanzhao, Tongbai, Nanyang, Songxian, Tanghe, Yiyang, Xinye, and Xin'an counties have suffered bandit disasters and wars, with unspeakable carnage. Survivors are unable to care for their fathers and sons, brothers and wives are scattered, and they are unlikely to survive until morning or evening. They will soon be swallowed up by the ravines. In Songxian, Xinan, Xiangxiang, Wuyang, and Lushi counties, there has been hail and rain, and in Nanyang and Xinyang, heavy rain has caused disasters. These dozens of counties are suffering from water, fire, and war, and it is difficult to care for the present. The loss of property and food is beyond mention. What is even more bizarre is that the Zichuan County Government of Henan Province reported by express mail that the county borders Shaanxi and has many mountains and few fields. It was originally a war zone, and its vitality has been exhausted. Starting from June 28th, there were weeks of torrential rain, and mountain floods broke out. The height of the water was actually fifteen or sixteen zhang. According to villagers, when the flood occurred, they saw a unicorn with a horn over seven chi high, its back above the water, bright red like cinnabar. There was also a thing with its head two zhang above the water, flowing downstream like a galloping horse. It was also said that a few days before the rain in Dalianyu Xiangtan, there was a continuous loud noise day and night, shocking the residents, and in the fields, they picked up an earthen egg, as big as a stone roller, peeled open six layers, and yellow soup flowed inside, and it was not known what it was. Although water monsters are not credible, the villagers have actually seen them and dare not withhold them from their superiors. With such disasters, the people will all die in the ravines. The only thing to rely on for relief is a glimmer of hope. The county received an emergency relief of three thousand yuan from your association eighteen years ago, saving countless disaster victims. Now, a strange disaster has occurred again. We only hope that your association will save people thoroughly, issue tickets, and allocate funds to bring the dead back to life. We are weeping and wailing, and we don't know what to say. The association has received successive reports of strange disasters from Anhui, Henan, and other provinces. Letters are flying in like snowflakes, with a dozen arriving every day. Recently, the heavy rain has not stopped, and floods have occurred again in various counties of Jiangsu Province. It is estimated that there are about two or three hundred counties in the country that have reported or have not yet reported disasters. With such severe natural disasters, the association is truly unable to start. The lonely survivors are crying and have no tears.

Chen Miaofu Stabbed

At about 9:10 PM last night, Chen Miaofu, a boatman from Pudong, 21 years old, and a pancake shop owner, Mr. Jia, gathered many people at the Xinglong Garden Teahouse on Xiamen Road to reason. Unexpectedly, they disagreed, and Mr. Jia's side immediately took out a pistol to intimidate them. Chen's friends all looked at each other in dismay and had to run away. Mr. Jia grabbed Chen Miaofu and beat him severely, stabbing Chen's chest, face, and head severely. The murderer then left in a swagger. After the injury, Western Patrol No. 259 arrived and took him to Renji Hospital for treatment by car.
