▲Tea and Snacks Trade Union of the Two-Line Beijing-Hangzhou Section: The Railway Bureau denied using the name of the trade union to sign the agreement for contracting the tea and snacks on the Shanghai-Hangzhou passenger cars. In order to seek a proper solution and cope with the situation, the union held an emergency meeting of all member representatives on the 25th. Comrade Wang Wei from the special party department of the two lines attended to guide the meeting. Xu Renyi was publicly elected as the chairman, and he reported on the process of petitioning the party department and negotiating with the Railway Bureau, as well as the recent claim by the Railway Bureau that the labor union should organize a tea and snack production company in order to sign the agreement. It was reported to the party department and sent to the Railway Bureau for reference. If the Railway Bureau refuses to sign the agreement in the name of the production cooperative again, it obviously wants to put the workers to death and will fight with all their strength to achieve the final victory. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

(C) Take action in unison with the Anti-Japanese and Overseas Chinese Support Association and send personnel to participate, and will not stop until the goals of abolishing the extraterritorial rights of the Japanese, punishing the murderers, apologizing, compensating, and recovering the concession are achieved. (5) The Loading and Unloading Union of Suzhou Station sent a letter requesting to send personnel to participate in the association's anniversary celebration. Resolution: Recommend Li Ganrong and Yu Yapu to participate. (6) How should we negotiate with Dingtong Company to stop paying the two-cent labor fee? Resolution: Check that the company automatically gave more commissions, which has nothing to do with the union. Now the company suddenly uses this to threaten and stop paying the labor fee, which is inappropriate. In addition to sending a letter to the Chinese stationmaster for negotiation, if there is no satisfactory solution, we can only strive for it unanimously based on reason. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Shanghai is Truly Dangerous: A Country Girl Nearly Falls into a Pit of Fire

▲Rickshaw Puller Suddenly Has Bad Intentions

▲Wuxi Woman Nearly Falls Victim to a Plot

▲Thin and Fat Rogues Use Evasive Language

▲Guangdong Brothel Owner Once Investigates

Zhuang Zhenying, a woman from Wuxi, is twenty-nine years old and has a slightly attractive appearance. Because she lived with her stepmother in Qingguo Lane in her hometown, she was often abused. Her father, Zhuang Zhenbao, works as a partner in the Zhufu Chang Iron Shop on Wuchang Road in Hongkou, Shanghai. Zhenying took the Shanghai-Ningbo train to Shanghai the morning before yesterday to find her father, but being unfamiliar with the place, she did not know where Wuchang Road was. She mistakenly walked to Wuma Road, and feeling tired, she hired a rickshaw pulled by Zhu Debiao, a Jiangbei native, asking him to take her to the iron factory on Wuchang Road. Passing Peng Road, she happened to be seen by Gu Ziquan, a fellow villager, who inquired about her situation. He advised her to return home because

There are many bad people in Shanghai, and it is very dangerous. If she is afraid of her stepmother's abuse, she can stay at his house temporarily and look for work in a silk factory, asking her to take the train back home at the North Railway Station. However, the details were heard by the rickshaw puller Zhu Debiao, who suddenly had bad intentions. He dragged Zhenying to the Xian Road area and walked slowly, intending to

Plan to sell her off, but Zhenying also suddenly changed her mind and did not want to return home. She asked Zhu Debiao to go to Wuchang Road to find her father. The rickshaw puller Zhu heard her words and felt it was just what he wanted. He stopped at the entrance of the Xian Inn at No. 1911 on that road and told Zhenying to stay at the inn temporarily. Then, the rogue Tongji Sang Xiaorizi and Xu Erhuzi explained the origin of Zhenying to the innkeeper, using the false name of Guo Baoshan, and arranged for her to stay in Room 20,

Falsely claiming to find her father on her behalf. However, Sang and Xu saw that Zhenying was young, ignorant, and pretty. Each had intentions of taking advantage of her. When Xu waited for Sang to leave the room, he said to Zhenying, "If you marry me, I will buy you a silk cheongsam to wear, buy you high-heeled leather shoes to wear, and give you a gold ring to wear," coaxing her in every way. Zhenying lowered her head and did not speak. After a while, Xu left and Sang entered, also saying to Zhenying, "I don't have a wife yet. If you agree to follow me, I will buy you beautiful clothes and take you to Xinxin Amusement Park." Soon, Zhu Debiao returned and advised Zhenying,

If you love a fat man, you should marry Xu Lang. If you love a thin man, you should marry Sang Lang. It's up to you to choose. If things work out, I will benefit. Please help me. But Zhenying did not answer. They knew that she was unwilling and could not be forced. After lunch, they went to the Guangdong brothel at No. 1167 on the same road and told the brothel owner Chen Ali that there was a woman from Wuxi, Zhuang Zhenying, in the Xian Inn who was willing to work as a prostitute. They asked her to observe her appearance, and if she was suitable, they would discuss the price. Madam Chen and a guest named Guang Sheng went to the inn at about 4:00 PM,

Examining Zhenying's appearance, once, and briefly talking to Zhu, Sang, and Xu, but they could not resolve the matter and left. At about 7:00 PM, Huatan An Siban and Zhao Lianbi from the Hongkou Police Station went to the inn to check the passengers. When they arrived at Room 20, they saw a woman and three men inside, and their behavior was suspicious. They arrested the three men and asked Zhenying about the situation. They went to the Guangdong brothel and arrested the brothel owner Chen Aliu, and took them to the police station for detention. The next morning, they were escorted to the Third Court of the Special Court. Lawyer Li Zhishan, the representative of the police station, stated the case and asked for a strict investigation. Then, the woman Zhuang Zhenying

Testified on the circumstances, and her father, Zhuang Zhenbao, also claimed to be working as a buyer of old goods at the Zhufu Chang Iron Shop on Wuchang Road. His hometown is Zhenjiang, and Zhenying was born to his former wife. She came to Shanghai to find him, and he knew nothing about it. It was only after the police detectives notified him. Zhenying's childhood name is Zhaodi, and there are still his old mother and stepmother in his family. Zhang Axiang, the tea waiter at the Xian Inn, also claimed that the woman Zhuang Zhenying and the three defendants Zhu Sangchu arrived at the same time yesterday morning and opened Room 20.

I don't know their intentions. The room was opened under the false name of Guo Baoshan, and I don't know anything else. The three defendants, Zhu, Sang, and Xu, were evasive in their confessions, denying that they had conspired to sell Zhenying into prostitution. However, Guangdong woman Xu Aliu confessed that she did not know any of the three men, Zhu, etc. She did go to the inn with Guang Sheng at the time and did not want to buy Zhenying for prostitution. She is not a brothel owner, but a helper in that place, and she begged for understanding. Judge Xiao Xieffen reviewed the confessions and ordered them to be returned to prison for sentencing on a fixed date. The woman Zhenying was taken back by her father Zhuang Zhenbao.

A Chorus of Bitter Rain

▲Minhang Already Shows Signs of Disaster

▲Old Farmers Eagerly Await Sunny Skies

▲Observatory Reports Rainfall: Lately, Continuous Rainfall... The mildewed rain causes low-lying areas to become inundated. People lament the rain, and signs of famine have emerged. Not only is the rain heavy, unseen in many years, but occurring during the hot summer, it has lasted for ten days, bringing a chill like deep autumn, which is rare even among the elders. According to records from the Xujiahui Observatory, from the 18th to the 25th, the rainfall in eight days totaled seven inches, nearly one-seventh of the annual rainfall. From New Year's Day to the present, it has totaled 37.71 inches. Records from the past 58 years show an average rainfall of only 27.53 inches during the same period, while this year has exceeded the average by more than ten inches. It is no wonder that rivers in various places are full and reports of flooding are frequent.

▲Signs of Disaster Already Seen in Minhang Town: Wu Jingqing, the district head of Minhang Town, recently reported to the county government on behalf of the district's farmers, saying that the cool and rainy weather has already shown signs of disaster, and requested that relief measures be planned in advance. The report stated that since the beginning of summer, the weather in the district has been drastically changing, with temperatures dropping, followed by heavy rain that has lasted for ten days. The rainfall has suddenly increased by two to three feet, causing cotton fields to be flooded and overgrown with weeds, while the rice paddies have also suffered from the unusual cold, slowing their growth. Such a situation has been seen only in the past decade or so. If the cold rain does not stop, it will inevitably lead to famine. The people, already in dire straits after years of disaster and civil unrest, are feeling extremely desolate. It is difficult to bear further suffering. In addition to personally comforting the village heads and encouraging the people to listen to fate and wait quietly for the weather to clear, it is appropriate to truthfully report the cold and rainy conditions and request your superiors to review and plan for relief, for the sake of public convenience.

▲Old Farmers Eagerly Await Sunny Skies: In the four southwestern rural areas of this city, cotton fields account for 70%, bean fields for 20%, and rice paddies for 10%. Previously, due to many days of rain, the higher terrain prevented flooding. However, because the cotton fields were too wet to weed, farmers were busy pulling weeds in the fields. The bean and rice crops had not suffered significant damage. Unexpectedly, since yesterday, torrential rain has fallen, and the water in the ditches has connected with the farmland. Yesterday, we saw that low-lying fields in the Caoxing, Pufa districts of this city, and the Zhuanbei and Maqiao areas of Shanghai County, had become inundated. The water level was two to three inches above the ground, causing the cotton fields, already plagued by weeds, to suffer further flooding. Farmers, with no hope for the autumn harvest, were lamenting to the heavens. According to the old farmers, they hope that the weather will clear immediately and the accumulated water will recede quickly. However, the cotton fields have already suffered more than half the damage, and most of the bean seedlings have been submerged and cannot be revived. If the rain continues, it is feared that it will lead to a major famine like the Tongzhi era of the Qing Dynasty.

▲Farmhouses Collapsed by Wind and Water: The previous night, thunder and lightning were intertwined, and the gale was even stronger. In the southwestern rural areas of this city, such as Caoxing, Pu, Song, and villages along the western edge to Qibao, farmhouses were collapsing everywhere due to wind and water. Most of these farmers' houses are old and dilapidated, and because of the long period of rain, they have become damp and unstable. The pillars are shaking, and they cannot withstand heavy rain and gales. Alas, our farmers, who have toiled all year round, have no hope for the autumn harvest, and have suffered the tragedy of collapsed houses. People have no place to live, like birds with overturned nests. We now know that the local officials in charge of rural affairs are inspecting the disaster situation and reporting to their superiors.

▲Navigation Between Kunshan and Taicang Interrupted: There used to be regular liners between Kunshan and Taicang, and between Taicang and Anting. Recently, due to the sudden rise in river water, the bridges are close to the water surface, and ships cannot pass. In addition, the riverbanks in various places have collapsed, making navigation quite dangerous. Passengers to the inland ports have no way to connect with the trains. Therefore, Taicang, Louqin, Yu Da, Guangli, and other shipping companies have implemented temporary remedial measures, opening the Shaxi-Taicang route. It departs from Shaxi at 7:00 AM every day, arrives in Taicang at 9:00 AM, and connects with the Tai-Liu route at 4:30 PM, returning to Shaxi. The Tai-Liu route departs from Taicang at 9:30 AM every day, arrives at Liuhe at 12:30 PM, connects with the Shanghai-Taicang long-distance bus, departs from Liuhe at 1:30 PM and returns to Taicang at 4:30 PM, connecting with the Shaxi route, so that passengers can continue their journey.

New Rules for the Shanghai Race Club's Grand Champagne Lottery

▲To Be Implemented This Autumn

The Shanghai Times reports that the Shanghai Race Club has recently issued a notice to its members, stating that it plans to change the Grand Champagne lottery for the spring and autumn seasons, merging the A and B types, issuing a total of 125,000 numbers, each priced at ten yuan, and expanding the number of prizes to 626. The first, second, and third prizes will all have double numbers. If all tickets are sold, the first prize will be 210,000 yuan, the second prize 60,000 yuan, and the third prize 30,000 yuan. Numbers drawn for qualified horses will be the fourth prize, totaling 120 numbers, each receiving approximately 1,250 yuan. Numbers drawn for unqualified horses will be the fifth prize, totaling 500 numbers, each receiving approximately 500 yuan. In the future, only numbers will be issued, not physical tickets. Each session will have a subscription list for members to purchase. These new rules are expected to be implemented this autumn.

The Truth About the Municipal Government's Land Acquisition

This time, in the municipal district's land bidding, Shanghai Bank acquired twenty plots, totaling more than three hundred acres. To others, it may seem that the bank acquired a disproportionate amount of land, but in fact, it was a joint trust acquisition by a group. According to the regulations for this land bidding, the municipal government initially feared that no one would be interested, so it initially bid for more than eight hundred acres. By 7:00 AM, more than three hundred people had arrived, and soon, several hundred more people came. Each person wanted to acquire fifty or one to two hundred acres. This exceeded the municipal government's expectations. At that time, because there was little land and many people, it was impossible to allocate it. The mayor was consulted, and it was decided to use a lottery system. Those who drew the first ticket would be given priority to acquire land, but they had to pay a quarter of the deposit on the spot. If there was land left over, those who drew the second ticket would acquire it, and so on, until all the land was sold. After this method was announced, those with quick minds, fearing that they would not draw a ticket, were completely disappointed. They temporarily sought acquaintances and formed groups, along with groups from various companies, totaling more than ten groups. Shanghai Bank, as the first to support the municipal government's plan to revitalize the central district, had sent personnel to conduct detailed investigations in the area several times in advance. On that day, the bank also sent personnel to acquire land. The groups temporarily elected the bank as their representative, specifying the number of acres they wanted to acquire. No matter who drew the ticket, it had to be allocated openly. A certain gentleman who drew the first ticket did not have enough cash and left after acquiring one plot. The second ticket happened to be drawn by a member of this group. The bank, therefore, represented the group and acquired twenty plots. It is now heard that the groups have been allocated more than three hundred acres, while Shanghai Bank itself only acquired forty-three acres, half of which has been sold to its staff for the construction of housing, so that staff can live together in unity, and the other half is planned for the construction of municipal housing to revitalize the city's commercial district, which is still in the planning stage. The bank's plan is purely to support the municipal government's efforts to promote the prosperity of the Chinese business district and has no intention of profiting. The municipal government's creation of this great policy, which has gained the trust of the citizens, is also unprecedented. However, since the citizens have considerable faith in the municipal government, the municipal government should also exert its strength to seek happiness for the residents. It is hoped that in the future, all municipal matters in the area, such as roads, ditches, security, and sanitation, will satisfy the people and live up to their expectations.

Construction of Heping Road to Begin Early Next Month

The municipal authorities' plan to rebuild Zhaojia Road as Heping Road, opening up Yi Lane and directly connecting to Route Lafayette to the west, has been under investigation by the Public Works Bureau for years, identifying municipal properties along the route that are obstructing the project. Around August last year, the Municipal Public Works Bureau ordered more than twenty owners and residents along the route to find new locations and relocate, demolishing the old houses. The bureau also bought them at the appraised market price. The demolition of the old houses along the route is expected to be completed by the end of this month, and construction will begin in early August. The leveling of the ground will be carried out by the Municipal Public Works Bureau, hiring regular workers to construct the surface, which will be paved with asphalt. It is estimated that the project will be completed within three months. After the completion of this project, which will connect the eastern end of Zhaojia Road to the Great Pier Street, the bureau will continue with the eastern section, renovating Great Pier Street, directly reaching the Bund of the Huangpu River. After the entire route is completed, the original road names will be abolished and completely renamed Heping Road.

Minutes of the Founding Meeting of the Dayong Rubber Company

Yesterday, the Dayong Rubber Company held its founding meeting at No. 144, East Seward Road. The Social Affairs Bureau sent Yu Tianbi to supervise the meeting. A total of 1,729 shares were represented. The meeting began at 3:00 PM, observing due protocol. The shareholders elected Jian Yingfu as the chairman. The chairman reported on the progress of the preparations, stating that the company was initiated in the autumn of 1930, and began soliciting shares in November of the same year. A factory site was leased at No. 30, Dissway Road, Central Hongqiao. It was originally planned to raise 100,000 yuan in shares, which would be the responsibility of the promoters to raise. Later, because the products were welcomed by customers and supply could not meet demand, the original capital was insufficient for development, so it was changed to 200,000 yuan. Therefore, machinery was purchased and raw materials were added, and after several months of progress, the preparations were completed. Construction began at the end of March, manufacturing sports shoes. In March and April, 53,000 pairs were produced, in May 45,000 pairs were produced, and in June 75,000 pairs were produced. Because there was too much demand for women's shoes on the market, printed women's shoes were added. The daily output still could not meet demand. At the beginning of operation, the output and sales had such results, which is truly a consolation to our shareholders. At present, all the machinery in the factory has been installed, including one large-sized rolling machine and four small-sized rolling machines. There are also two small-sized rolling machines that will be installed during the day. After that, the daily output will be 200 dozen sports shoes, 150 dozen women's shoes, and 50 dozen rubber-soled basketball shoes. As for sales, Shunfa and Xinyi are the general managers, who guarantee sales on a monthly basis. This is a brief overview of the preparations and the current business situation. Next, the draft articles of association were discussed. The chairman read them item by item, made slight revisions, and the rest were passed. The chairman then asked the shareholders to vote to elect directors and supervisors. The shareholders elected Pan Ziyi and Wu Shuping as supervisors and ballot counters. The results of the ballot count were that Chen Lianbo, Jian Yujie, Jian Yingfu, Lao Jingxiu, Li Hui, Zeng Gongluo, Shen Ziliang, Liu Weijun, and Gong Yuting were elected as directors, and Jian Qingman and Pan Ziyi were elected as supervisors. The meeting adjourned at 5:00 PM.

Car Crash Death Case

▲Driver Sentenced to Three Months Imprisonment

Zhao Changjiang, a Yangzhou native working as a driver for the Zhang Faji Transportation Company at No. 274, Mowhai Road, was driving truck No. 17015 on the 15th of this month at around 6:00 AM. Due to the driver's carelessness, he ran over a six-year-old boy named Jin Hai, the son of a Guizhou woman Zhang Shenshi, near the Xiaocai Chang on Hankow Road. The boy was injured in the waist and died. Chinese police officer No. 2696 and Western police officer No. 25 from the Hongkou police station arrived and detained Zhao for questioning and imprisonment in the Special District Court. Yesterday, Judge Feng Shide opened the Third Court for hearing. According to the presentation of the case by lawyer Li Zhishan from the police station, and the investigation during the adjournment, it was determined that the defendant was driving in violation of the route, which caused the child to be run over and killed. At that time, the right wheel rolled over the child's waist, and he did not stop for more than twenty feet, showing that he was driving very fast. The drawn map of the accident site was presented for inspection. According to the testimony of the woman Zhang Shenshi, she was leading her son Jin Hai from north to south, and the defendant's car was speeding from east to west without honking its horn. First, he knocked me down, and then ran over Jin Hai, killing him, and did not stop. She also hired a lawyer to argue, requesting punishment of the defendant, and for the civil part, requested compensation for consolation money of 10,000 yuan. The defendant firmly stated that he was not driving fast at the time and did not see the child fall to the ground. He only knew after the worker on the car told him. The rest of the testimony was evasive. He also hired a lawyer to defend him. After reviewing the testimony, Judge Feng sentenced Zhao Changjiang to three months in prison. The number of days of detention before the judgment was final will be deducted at the rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. The civil lawsuit filed by the plaintiff will be transferred to the civil court for trial.

Husband and Wife Quarrel, Jump into the Huangpu River

▲Fortunately, Shu Wengshi Did Not Die

Yesterday morning at around 9:00 AM, the ferry from the Fenshan Wharf in Pudong, carrying about 20 men and women passengers from Puxi, returned to Pudong. Unexpectedly, after sailing to the middle of the river, a middle-aged woman among the passengers threw herself into the river to commit suicide. Her body sank and floated again. The boatman managed to rescue her and sent her to the police station at the pier, who took her to the Fourth Detachment of the Police. She changed her wet clothes and was transferred to the Third District of the Lan Nidu Public Security Bureau. According to the woman's statement, her name is Shu Wengshi, she is 28 years old, from Ningbo, and lives at No. 282, Gongping Road, Hongkou. Her husband's name is Shu Xinyou, and she has an eight-year-old son. Because the husband and wife were not in harmony, she was abused by her husband, unable to bear the pain, so she embraced pessimism and jumped into the river to commit suicide. Unfortunately, she was rescued. The district chief, considering that her family lived in the concession, ordered the woman to be transferred to the headquarters in the afternoon.

A Ha-Ha Laugh Almost Leads to Death

▲Song Guangfu Punches Li Jiafa

Li Jiafa, a Ningbo native, 40 years old, rented a room at No. 51, Dongchang Road, Pudong, and made a living by setting up a stall by the roadside. Yesterday morning, Song Guangfu's manure cart passed by. Li was unable to avoid it and was hit by the cart, but he was not seriously injured. Unexpectedly, the two started arguing and refused to give in, grabbing and beating each other. Song suddenly punched Li hard in the waist. Li laughed loudly, and his face immediately turned white. He fell to the ground, barely breathing. After a few minutes, he suddenly recovered, groaning incessantly. The police arrived and took Song Guangfu and the injured Li Jiafa to the Third District. The district chief ordered Song to be temporarily detained, and Li was sent to Pudong Hospital for treatment. It is heard that his injuries are severe and he may be in danger of losing his life.

Two Laborers Electrocuted

Chen Bangshan, a 27-year-old man from Ningbo, residing at No. 14 Jiuru Lane, Qiujiang Road, Zhabei, worked as a painter at Huamei Advertising Company on Ningbo Road. Yesterday morning, around 9:50 AM, the company sent him to paint an advertising billboard on the roof north of Pintang Bridge. It was drizzling, and he accidentally touched a live electrical wire. His body was stuck to the power pole. A patrolman from Post No. 3166 saw this and immediately broke the wooden pole to free him. He fell to the ground, injuring his head, shoulders, and feet. He was rushed to Tongren Hospital for treatment, but to no avail. He died at around 3 PM. The hospital transferred the body to the forensic examination office on Faelun Road, and the court was notified for investigation.

Yang Yongqing, a 26-year-old worker at Yihe Cotton Mill in Yangshupu, was working on machinery yesterday at noon when he accidentally touched an electric current and died. Fire trucks later transported his body to the forensic examination office for investigation.

Fifty-Seven-Year-Old Man Frauds and Defiles Young Girl

▲Yu Zhenxiao Flees Far Away

The case of Yu Zhenxiao, a 57-year-old owner of Yida and other lumber companies, and his younger brother Yu Zibiao, who used fraudulent means to seduce and defile Liang Junzhen, a 17-year-old girl, has led the District Court to order the police chief to issue an arrest warrant. Based on the evidence presented by the plaintiff, an investigation was conducted. At the Fenghuang Hotel, it was confirmed that Yu Zibiao had indeed seduced the girl, and a report was submitted. The case file has been attached. The police chief has been instructed to arrest and bring the suspects to justice. Furthermore, a letter has been sent to the various organizations in the foreign concessions, requesting their cooperation in the arrest to uphold public morals.

Coal Handler Falls into River and Drowns

▲Shi Bu San's Body Retrieved

The day before yesterday afternoon, while workers were unloading coal at the Taikoo Wharf in Pudong, a laborer carrying coal down from the ship accidentally slipped off the gangplank and fell into the river. He immediately sank and drowned. Another laborer, Wang Fengxiang, recognized him as Shi Bu San from Shanyang, residing at No. 26 Tianbao Lane, behind the Garden Stone Bridge in Pudong. Wang notified Shi’s wife, Madam Guan, who arrived at the scene to search for the body but could not find it. She cried bitterly and accused the foreman, Jiang Longxi, of using an unstable gangplank, causing her husband to fall into the river and drown. She harassed Jiang relentlessly. The patrol police stationed at the wharf took Jiang and Madam Guan to the Third District. Shi’s body was recovered with a grappling hook in the evening. Yesterday, the comprador of the wharf intervened and mediated. Considering Shi's poor financial situation and the pitiful circumstances, they provided clothing, a coffin, and a certain amount of compensation to the family. The case was closed, and foreman Jiang Longxi was released on bail.

Qibao Town After the Fire

Qibao Town, west of Shanghai, suffered a devastating fire on the night of the 18th of this month, caused by the carelessness of Chengchang Foreign Goods Store, which spread to more than twenty neighboring businesses, including Hengsheng Clothing Store. The losses are estimated at around 100,000 taels of silver, marking a significant disaster for the town. Furthermore, very few stores had fire insurance, adding to the financial burden. However, as the town has been incorporated into the city, it cannot be left desolate. The business owners have already begun reconstruction, building the newest style of shops. Merchants can reserve rentals or customize designs in advance. The construction of the town will gradually become modern.

Traditional Chinese Medicine Doctor Yu Peiyuan Revises Consultation Regulations

For impoverished patients, free consultations are available every morning from 7:00 AM to 8:00 AM. Dr. Yu's residence is located at No. 3, Sande Lane, Jiaochangshao, outside Xiaonanmen.

Letter to the Editor

Dear Editor,

Regarding the news of the assassination attempt on Vice President Song of the Executive Yuan at the North Railway Station on the 23rd of this month, as reported by various newspapers, and the arrest warrant issued by the Public Security Bureau today, there is much misunderstanding about the railway police's management of station security and the division of authority between the Public Security Bureau and the railway police. The checking of travelers at the three main entrances of the North Station (east, west, and south) has always been the responsibility of soldiers from the Zhejiang-Shanghai Garrison Command and police officers from the Fifth District of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau. The Station Inspection Office of the Garrison Command was recently abolished. On July 2nd, Order No. 1109 of the Garrison Command clearly stipulated that the task of checking travelers at the station be assigned to police officers from the Public Security Bureau. On the 22nd, when Vice President Song arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing, we did not receive a telegram due to a disruption in the railway telegraph lines. Only when the night train arrived did we see Vice President Song disembark. We immediately dispatched Police Chief Zhao Xinzong and Police Officer Lu Youcai to provide protection. When the assassin threw the bomb, the railway police had no firearms and could not retaliate with bare hands. They closely followed and protected Vice President Song, assisting him to quickly ascend to the second floor of the Management Bureau to take refuge. Vice President Song should still remember the collar badges and cap emblems of the railway police protecting him, as well as his inquiries to me about the situation. At that time, in addition to sending police to protect Vice President Song, I also summoned the off-duty police officers to the station to supervise and maintain order and to apprehend the assassin. However, at that time, four passenger trains were departing from our station, and the night express train from Nanjing was arriving, with passengers crowding the station. Upon hearing the alarm, they fled in confusion, disrupting order. With the smoke and chaos, it was impossible to identify the assassin's true identity, allowing the assassin to abandon his weapon and escape in the confusion, which is a great regret. After the incident, we recovered one Mauser pistol, two Browning pistols, and one unexploded bomb at the station. It is inconceivable that the assassin(s) could enter the station, given the strict inspection of prohibited items at the three main entrances. The railway police serving at the station, including those at the platforms and ticket offices, number less than ten, and are dedicated to maintaining order within the station and suppressing petty criminals. Although we were fortunate to protect Vice President Song's safety in this shooting incident, our lack of pre-emptive protection was due to insufficient police strength and our inability to resist heavily armed bandits with bare hands. Ultimately, we are ashamed of dereliction of duty. We have submitted a request to our superiors to take responsibility for the lapse. The railway police and the public security police are both police forces, and our duties are the same. The police officers from the Fourth and Fifth Districts of the Public Security Bureau have always worked in harmony and mutual support when handling incidents at the station, and there has never been a so-called issue of division of authority. The report that only one public security police officer was checking travelers at the station, with the rest at the Baoshan Road intersection, is somewhat inaccurate. This matter concerns the division of authority and the truth of the situation. I am therefore informing you of the station's historical situation and the facts of the incident, hoping that you will publish this to ensure accuracy and to address public concerns.

Sincerely,

He Jinxiu, Police Chief of the First Section of the Nanjing-Shanghai Railway, July 26th.

Sports

Sensation in Paris: Davis Cup Final, Britain Ties at Two-Two

▲Yesterday's Singles: Austin Wins Over Borotra ▲

▲Second Day Doubles: French Team Wins Over British Team ▲

▲Championship Depends on Results of Perry vs. Cochet ▲

丨Yesterday's Singles Results丨

Paris, 26th - Davis Cup final. In the third day of singles, Britain's Austin defeated France's Borotra, 7-5, 6-3, 3-6, 7-5. In the first set, Borotra took an early lead of 3-0. Austin persisted and won the second set with short and long shots. In the third set, they were tied at 3-3 before Borotra won. In the final set, Austin won with powerful shots. After three days, Britain and France are tied at two-two. Who will win the championship depends on the results of Perry vs. Cochet.

丨Second Day Doubles丨

Paris, 25th - Davis Cup tennis, Britain vs. France, in the final for the championship. Today, the second day, the French doubles team won 3-1 against the British team, giving France a 2-1 lead. The outcome is still uncertain. The final two singles matches are evenly matched, and it is impossible to predict the winners before the match. The crowd was larger than on the first day. After the rain, the court was covered with sand.

▲French Doubles Victory Over Britain's Results

Cochet and Brugnon (France) 6-1, 5-7, 6-3, 8-6 beat Hughes and Kingsley (Britain)

Maintaining Strength, Britain Changes Strategy

The British doubles team has always been Perry and Hughes. However, Perry also has to play singles, holding two positions, and has to compete for three consecutive days. His strength will inevitably be greatly affected on the third day of singles. Perry's final singles match will also be against the strong Cochet. Therefore, team leader Barat changed his strategy, having Kingsley replace Perry in the doubles match, knowing that the doubles match would inevitably be lost to France. This was to preserve Perry's strength and prepare for a decisive battle with Cochet.

▲British Doubles Not Inferior

The Hughes and Kingsley doubles team was not inferior in strength. In the second set, they fought for twelve games and won 7-5. In the final set, they also fought hard for fourteen games, but unfortunately lost 6-8. The struggle was extremely fierce.

Zhou Xianyan, Li Ning, Feng Yunyou, Chen Pu, Bili Cao, Lidu, Chen Zhenhe, Xiao Gaoshan Nu, Da Gaoshan Nu, Chen Jiaqiu, Victor

▲Combined Team Takes an Early Lead

Appraising the Japanese University of Commerce's Boasted First-Class Basketball Team (Lu Zhong'en)

丨Combat Strength Still Strong丨Lacking in Artistic Aspects丨

▲Five Losses and Two Wins in Seven Matches丨A Mediocre Team After All

The University of Commerce basketball team, boasting itself as Japan's first-class, has come to Shanghai to challenge local teams seven times. Comparing its performance in the past matches with the strength of Shanghai's teams, it can only be considered mediocre. However, the team's combativeness is remarkably tenacious, worthy of praise. But in terms of artistic aspects, it still lacks refinement. Therefore, out of seven matches, it has won two and lost five. Now, I will briefly record my observations from each game for the readers to study.

(1) University of Commerce vs. Fan Hang: This was the first match for the University of Commerce. Fan Hang was unfortunately defeated due to incomplete personnel. On that evening, the University of Commerce did not appear exceptionally brilliant. Fan Hang's two guards were slightly weak, with errors frequently occurring in receiving and defense. As a result, Fan Hang unfortunately lost with a score of 34 to 31.

(2) University of Commerce vs. Eagle Team: In this match, the University of Commerce did not gain any advantage from beginning to end. Although the team fought fiercely, it missed many opportunities due to being too hasty. Shooting opportunities were often not grasped effectively. The three forwards of the Eagle Team were not seasoned veterans. Although Kong of Chizhi and Guangyi would lend their efforts, the audience generally felt there was no hope. Unexpectedly, after forty minutes of strenuous battle, the Eagle Team defeated the visiting team with a score of 34 to 25, a truly remarkable feat.

(3) University of Commerce vs. Artillery Team: The University of Commerce suddenly recovered its ability from the first night amidst a period of poor performance, overwhelming the Artillery Team. The Artillery Team consisted of skilled players, but their shooting skills were lacking, reducing their scoring opportunities. Ultimately, they could not achieve perfection, which was regrettable. At the end of the match, the University of Commerce secured its second victory with a score of 36 to 32.

(4) University of Commerce vs. Fudan United: Fudan United assembled a strong team composed of new and old students to resist the University of Commerce. The team's cooperation was commendable. Forwards Guo and Lu frequently attacked the enemy's basket, coupled with the inner defense's exhaustive efforts, finally repelling the enemy. The score was 26 to 19. In this match, both sides had many fouls, and the essence of the game was lost, making it somewhat flawed.

(5) University of Commerce vs. Red Light: Red Light was formed by merging Guanghua and the Red Team. The course of the battle was very similar to that against Fudan United. With an indomitable spirit and a stroke of luck, they seized the final victory. In this match, the University of Commerce appeared even more regressed than in the match against Fudan United. In the last six minutes, although it added the Far East warriors Ohashi and Ueda into the battle, it still ended in defeat. Poor shooting and the inability to adapt the offense to the situation were the biggest reasons for the Japanese team's repeated failures. In conclusion, Red Light 31, University of Commerce 27.

(6) University of Commerce vs. Chizhi: Chizhi, the champion of Jiangnan University, naturally had strength above that of the University of Commerce. Therefore, the University of Commerce exerted all its strength to cope. The competition between the two sides was very intense. The Chizhi team led all the way with its superior technique and accurate shooting. In the second half, University of Commerce unfortunately had its main player, Nagai, ejected from the game due to four fouls. Therefore, at the end of the match, the University of Commerce lost by twelve points (the score was 32 to 20). In this match, both sides were penalized a total of 28 times due to fierce competition, creating the highest number in the University of Commerce's challenge series.

(7) University of Commerce vs. Shanghai Chinese: The Shanghai Chinese basketball team, recognizing the immaturity of the University of Commerce's technique, decided to strive for variety in artistic aspects. The advantage of the University of Commerce lies entirely in its serious and persistent fighting spirit, charging straight ahead without any sense of change. Therefore, the Shanghai Chinese players embraced the principle of "I do not offend others" and used pure artistry to deal with the visiting team. In defense, recognizing the Japanese team's emphasis on close-range shots and basket rebounds, one side adopted the "Five Men Position Defence" method, while the other side closely monitored the Japanese team's only shooter, Mr. Nagai. In offense, one side used quick counterattacks (Quick Breaks) to attack unprepared opponents, while the other side used "Cut fns," "Bounce Pass," and shots within the free-throw area. The opposing team also talked about the same five-man defensive formation (Five Men Defence). If the University of Commerce had adopted the Shanghai Chinese's offensive techniques in the second half, it would not have lost by as many as thirty points.

In conclusion, the University of Commerce's expedition to Shanghai was far from what was expected. The skill of the so-called first-class team in Japan has been seen by us Chinese. We sincerely hope that Japan can send an invincible championship team to Shanghai next time to compete. Then the strength between China and Japan can be clearly understood.

The Allied forces launched a fierce attack like cannonballs. China's defense was not yet fully established. Suddenly facing a strong enemy, they were caught off guard, and the enemy broke through the central pass. The Portuguese player (Victor) was exceptionally brave, carrying the ball and flying in, taking advantage of the momentum to kick it diagonally. Chen at the goal was unable to save it in time. Thus, in less than five minutes, the Allied team first announced victory.

▲China Immediately Retaliates

China was caught off guard and conceded a goal. They were unwilling to let go and became as fierce as dragons and tigers, vowing to recover their territory. They fought fiercely for more than ten minutes, with no clear winner. Unexpectedly, trouble arose from a small incident. Li Ruchen secretly carried the ball, breaking through two lines of defense. Li Yi and Shuang Ma met the challenge, embracing into a ball. The ball flowed out from under Ma's belly. Lu Qiyuan was quick-eyed and quick-footed, and the ball flew like an arrow. Even the famous general Zhou Xianyan could do nothing. The score was tied.

▲Chinese Army Continues to Report Victory

After five minutes of switching positions and fighting again, the Allied army seemed to relax and lost the rhythm of passing, naturally giving others an opportunity. He Zuoxian was a good general and could not miss this opportunity, quickly assisting the front line to calmly carry out the attack. Mai Laodong went to the front line under orders, killing relentlessly, and Billy Cao lost his guard and was defeated. At the right time, he passed the ball from the middle, and the ball fell from the sky, directly attacking the goal. Sun Tie Tui (Jinshun) was in a favorable position and, abandoning his feet, used his head to strike diagonally, and the ball went into the net.

▲Dagaoshan Nu Scores a Goal

Not long after switching positions and fighting again, the Allied forces' military appearance was too strong. The five forwards lined up like wild geese and advanced bravely. China's central pass was broken, and the atmosphere suddenly became tense. Hai Jia Ball rode forward, full of energy, carrying the ball and flying in, like a dragon emerging from the water. Generals Huang and Liang met and engaged in a mixed battle. Chen immediately passed diagonally to the center forward. Dagaoshan Nu was originally a famous foreign general who seized the opportunity and regained the lost territory. His contribution was not small.

▲The Locomotive Actually Scores a Goal

China lost a goal unexpectedly. How could they be willing to have the meat in their mouths taken away? They urgently planned a counterattack and launched a series of attacks. Chen Pu kicked the ball in a hurry, and the Chinese army's attack was ineffective and retreated. The locomotive opened from the left pass for the second time, Billy Cao could not stop it, and directly approached the left corner and passed the ball straight down to the goal. The momentum was extremely urgent. Zhou Xianyan punched but could not stop it, and the ball directly penetrated the net. It was clear and beautiful.

▲Finally Tie the Score

The ball game reached this point, and the atmosphere suddenly became tense. Every move, forward or backward, won applause from ten thousand people. The Chinese ball team, with the record already at three to two, strictly defended their position, taking a defensive stance. The Allied team urgently deployed troops, trying to quickly recover their lost territory. Not long after, Chen Zhenhe carried the ball to attack, Chen Xipei came to meet him and tried to pounce, and the people and the ball rolled to the ground, embracing into a ball. Black Charcoal wanted to kick, but Xipei refused to let go. The referee blew a whistle, and the Allied team was relieved, judging it as a "fair ball." The ball was thrown into the air to see who would get it first. Black Charcoal was like a fish in the net and could not be allowed to escape. He pushed away with one foot, and the ball flew as ordered. Sure enough, the heavens did not fail those who worked hard, and he finally won the final victory. Soon after, the battle whistle blew, and the battle curtain slowly fell. A pair of inseparable friends fought to a draw, and they came as a team and left as a team.

▲Renovation of Zhongshan Gate in Nanjing

The Nanjing Municipal Bureau of Public Works, considering the large number of visitors to the National Games, found the Zhongshan Gate, which they must pass through, to be very narrow, and transportation may be inconvenient. Therefore, the city gate will be rebuilt, changing one to three, with work to be completed before the Double Tenth Festival. From our local area.

Zhaoji Middle School Applies for Registration

Zhaoji Middle School had previously submitted applications to the Municipal Bureau of Education in the years of the Republic 17 and 19 for approval to operate a complete middle school. This spring, Father Lao moved the school to Jisi Feier Road. Now, the school board has submitted an application for school registration and it is rumored that the first enrollment of new students for the 20th year will be held on August 10.

Zhengfeng Middle School Board of Directors Expanded

Since Dr. Huang Sen became the principal of Zhengfeng Middle School on Gordon Road, the school's affairs and academics have been renewed. This semester, Gu Nanqun, Qian Yuchen, Pu Jizhong, and Zai Zhiqing have been newly appointed as school board members, and the matter has been submitted to the Municipal Bureau of Education for record. All the school board members are prominent business figures in Shanghai. It is rumored that the school has purchased more than ten acres of school land near the central district.

Shanggong School Adds Teachers

Shanggong School on Baike Road, formerly Shanghai Gongxue, has been operating for fifteen years. It is rumored that the school has been approved by the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education to establish a summer school for tutoring. New student registrations have been very enthusiastic. The school is currently adding famous teachers and opening up classrooms, planning for expansion in the second half of the year.

Principal Zhou of Nanxiang Public School Resigns

Zhou Dinghua, the principal of Nanxiang Private Nanxiang Public School, has been in office for more than twenty years. He has planned carefully and spared no effort, from elementary school to complete elementary school, and from complete elementary school to adding a junior high school. There are now more than 800 students, the most in Jiading County. The school's facilities are complete, and its achievements are outstanding, praised by local people. This time, he resigned due to brain disease. Although the school council, school branch council, faculty and staff council, and parents of students have repeatedly tried to retain him, Principal Zhou's determination to resign was firm, and there was no possibility of reversal. Local people lamented this. It is now heard that the school branch council has scheduled a farewell party on August 9, and it is also rumored that various parties will make some expressions of appreciation.

Zhiming Elementary School Adds a Second Branch

Private Zhiming School is located at No. 19 Yaojia'an Lane, Zhaojia Road, Laoximen. The number of students is increasing day by day, and the school building cannot be expanded. Because Yan Hai Elementary School on Chuanxin Street, Laobeimen, has been closed, there is a deep fear that children nearby will feel inconvenienced and find it difficult to attend school. Therefore, the school will be divided into a second branch at the old site of Yan Hai, renovating the school building and organizing it. It is said that school will begin on September 1.

Special Article

A New Aspect of Chinese Education

丨Central Political School (I) Xingye

The strict curriculum, serious discipline, excellent school spirit, and rapid development of the Central Political School have gradually attracted the attention of society. This kind of school occupies a special position in the history of education, and its influence on the future politics of China will be considerable. I think that the general public in the country is happy to have an accurate and reliable understanding, so I have recorded it in detail for reference. According to the world's political schools, there are not many, and the most famous and only ones that can be counted are the French I'Fcocle des Sciences Politiques and the German Politische Hochschule. Both are university in nature and are in the same city as the University of Paris and the University of Berlin, and their level is the same. Coincidentally, the political school in Paris was established after the Franco-Prussian War in 1871 to seek political reform and restore France's lost international status after the Franco-Prussian War. The German political school was established after the Treaty of Paris in 1919, because at that time, the Germans only admitted that the previous war was not a military failure but a political failure. For the sake of political reform, in order to seek revival, the Central Political School of China happened to be established after the National Government made Nanjing its capital, when it was calling for the revival of the Chinese nation and the reform of Chinese politics. It is also the same university in level. Looking at the trajectory of its evolution, it is gradually tending towards being run as a French political school in particular.

When the National Government made Nanjing its capital, the Central Government felt the lack of practical workers, so it established the Central Party Affairs School. This school was the predecessor of the Central Political School. The training period of the Party Affairs School was one year. Although the level varied, many were university graduates and vocational school graduates. Soon after this class graduated, it was changed to the Central Political School, and the study period was combined into four years, recruiting graduates from registered high schools and university preparatory courses, and its level became the same as that of national universities. Moreover, strict enrollment is a special phenomenon of political schools. Now, the students in the first and second grades of the political school are selected from an average of fourteen people. Most of the professors are well-known figures at the time. Because the school is in the capital, in addition to full-time professors, it is also easier to hire professionals to serve as part-time lecturers. As far as the current situation is concerned, their treatment is higher than that of any university in the capital, and the qualifications for selection and appointment are also very strict. Originally, this school was divided into four departments: Administration, Finance, Local Autonomy, and Social Economy. Its classification was different from that of general universities. On January 1, 1920, after Luo Jialun returned to the school, he established the purpose of running the school as a French political school. He believed that this kind of division was still too broad, and if he wanted to cultivate specialized talents, he had to concentrate students' interests on the specialized schools they recognized. Otherwise, it would be the same as ordinary universities. On the one hand, it could not compare with foreign universities, so that students could have in-depth research on academic theories after graduation. On the other hand, it could not supply politics and society with practical needs. Everything could be done, but nothing could be done. Therefore, he set a fundamental plan to divide the departments into groups, so that students would have a need and object for their work in the subjects they wanted to study. Therefore, after determining the policy, he divided the original departments into groups. The Department of Administration was divided into three groups: General Administration, Law, and Diplomacy. The purpose of the Law Group was to cultivate judicial officers, prison officers, and personnel for administrative courts and supervisory courts. Because there were not many talents in China in the legal field, and after the abolition of consular jurisdiction in the future, the demand for judicial talents would be greater. In order to make the decisions of local courts in various places on civil and criminal lawsuits not subject to international public opinion, we need good judicial talents. The second is the General Administration Group, which focuses on the research of policy implementation and the knowledge of institutional management to increase administrative efficiency. The third is the Diplomacy Group, which focuses on the research of diplomatic issues and cultivates talents for embassies and consulates. The Law Group belongs to the Department of Administration purely as a historical evolution, and it may be established as a separate department in the future. Under the Department of Finance, two groups are set up: Financial Administration and Finance. The Financial Administration Group focuses on the implementation and planning of tax collection, tax forecasting, and auditing. The purpose of the Finance Group is to cultivate practical talents for monetary systems and national and public financial institutions. Further down is the Department of Local Autonomy, which is divided into four groups: Municipal Administration, Rural Administration, Land Administration, and Police Administration. The Municipal Administration Group focuses on urban design, police, public health, and relief issues. The Rural Administration Group focuses on rural administration, rural education, implementation of civil rights training, and forest protection issues. The Land Administration Group focuses on land surveying and registration, public land management, and the implementation of land law to cultivate talents for organizing national land. The Police Administration Group is to cultivate talents who can bear the responsibility of national public security. In addition to police administration, it also teaches sufficient legal knowledge and focuses on social investigation and statistics. The preparation of these two groups is more difficult, so they are temporarily postponed. The fourth is the Department of Social Economy, which is divided into four groups: Public Utilities, Cooperation, Statistics, and Industrial and Commercial Administration. The Public Utilities Group focuses on the management, operation, and supervision of public utilities. The Cooperation Group focuses on the guidance and operation of cooperative undertakings and related technologies. The Statistics Group focuses on the training of various statistical skills. The Industrial and Commercial Administration Group focuses on labor-capital arbitration, factory management, the implementation of factory supervision systems, and the improvement of foreign trade matters. This is the purpose of the establishment of each group and its teaching policy. By June of this year, with the permission of the Central Government, the Department of Education was added, divided into two groups: Educational Administration and Rural Education. The lack of educational administrative talents is already very obvious, and the need to promote rural education can be stated by those who speak about Chinese issues. The establishment of this department is also established to meet the needs of the country. The above is the situation of the school's undergraduate program. The undergraduate program is only up to the third grade, and there will be a fourth grade in the second half of the year, so the school has not yet had any graduates.

Free Talk

A Small Chronicle of the World

— Hai Ke

The Museum of Brains

The strangest museum in the world. It has now been established in Vienna, the capital of Austria. It is attached to a scientific academy that studies human intelligence. It specializes in displaying human brains. The museum has obtained many brains of past geniuses. And almost a thousand living geniuses have also promised to send their brains to the museum for display after their death. The average European male brain weighs forty-five taels, and the average female brain weighs forty taels. Generally speaking, the more intelligent a person is, the heavier their brain is. The brain of the great British poet Byron weighed sixty taels. The brain of the great German philosopher Kant weighed fifty-five taels. And the brain of the great Russian writer Turgenev exceeded them, weighing as much as sixty-seven taels. To know the weight of the brain, there is no need to weigh it on a scale. You only need to measure the size of the skull to know the weight of the brain accurately. If you compare the brains of ancient people with the brains of modern people, the difference in intelligence is very large. The brains of Javanese orangutans and savage races all over the world are very light. But the brains of people in several places in ancient France two or three thousand years ago who invented flint to make fire and people who painted beautiful murals in Spanish caves also weighed as much as the brains of modern people. This cannot be generalized. There is also an exception to the exception, which is the record of the heaviest brain in the world, weighing seventy-seven taels, but it belongs to an idiot. Isn't it strange?

A Nation Without Promise

— Zhou Cailiang

Since the Wanbaoshan incident, hundreds of our Korean-Chinese compatriots have been killed. The expression of national economic severance with Japan is one way of doing things when there is no other way. It is sighing to say that weak countries have no diplomacy. Still remember Cai Yuanpei's crazy saying, "Being pro-Japanese is certainly not possible. Hating Japan is also not appropriate. But knowing Japan is the most effective." For the Japanese, China is almost at their fingertips. But our countrymen know nothing about them. I think knowing Japan is important, but knowing Korea is also essential. But if you want to know people's strengths and weaknesses, you must experience it personally. My friend Mr. Pan has just returned from traveling in Korea and has many feelings. He told me the following. The great reason for the fall of Korea is only three greed. The first is greed for food. Because they are greedy for food, they only know how to consume and do not know how to produce. The second is greed for laziness. Because they are greedy for laziness, nothing can be done. The third is greed for money. Because they are greedy for money, they are blinded by greed and do not know there is a country. The Japanese know this and deliberately make it so, gradually using them as puppets to oppose China. This kind of nation without promise is willing to be a tiger's accomplice. It is not surprising. I sincerely hope that the Chinese who live in independent countries will quickly know the reason why and prevent it from happening. In that case, even if the Japanese are cunning, I am afraid they will have no way to use their skills.

Tidbits

— (Juan)

Economic severance with Japan is the only method we can use when we have no other choice. If we can't even do this, and we can't even persevere to the end, then it's true that what the ancients called "There is no greater sorrow than the death of the heart." There is also one important point, which is that those who preside over the inspection of goods must be selfless and upright. If they dare to accept a bribe of even one cent, it is tantamount to seeing Korean-Chinese compatriots being killed and then secretly eating the remaining pieces of meat and sipping the remaining blood. This kind of person is Chen Shubao, who has no heart or liver at all.

The Fun of History and Geography Tests

— Xue Qian

The purpose of having history and geography in schools is to understand the present by knowing the past. In fact, it is nothing more than understanding the process of life and the current situation. Therefore, except for universities that have specialized history and geography research, in middle and primary school students, it mostly belongs to common sense, which is necessary to know in fact, and should be included in the teaching materials. During this summer vacation, Shanghai Municipal Wuben Girls' Middle School recruited new students. In addition to testing Sanmin Zhuyi, Chinese, and mathematics, history and geography are one type of common sense, and of course, they are also included in the test. But as a result, there are many errors in the answers. For example, when asked what time period Confucius lived in, some filled in Tang Dynasty, and some filled in Song Dynasty, accounting for four or five tenths of the total. Those who filled in the Zhou Dynasty could still understand his era. As for those who filled in the Spring and Autumn period, there were only one or two tenths. Also, when asked about the names of the Seven Heroes, some filled in England, America, Germany, France, Japan, Italy, and Austria. It can be said to be a big mistake. It is already very funny to even fill in Tang Wu as peasant revolution. And the two sons of Sima Yi, one named ○ and one named ○, one student filled in Sima Qian and Sima Guang, which are eight or nine hundred years apart, so the error is extremely extreme. Even more laughable, the question asked who was the most resourceful person in the Three Kingdoms period, and one student filled in the three characters "Shi Yi Hao." At first glance, it was unknown what he meant. After careful consideration, I suddenly realized that it was Zhuge Liang's mistake. Also, with the five ports of the Treaty of Nanjing, anyone should know their locations. Who would have thought that some would not be able to name them, or they would be incomplete, or the names would be mostly wrong. It can also be seen that common sense is lacking. As for the central area of Shanghai City being in ○○○, some filled in Nanjing and some filled in Guangzhou, and they still do not know the recent situation. As for the seven coastal provinces and the three major basins of the headquarters, they are even less clear. I remember last year there was a question to list the names of China's four major railway lines. A student taking the high school exam answered one Huanghuogan, two Huogan, and three Chihuogan. To investigate why there was such a big mistake, I took the question paper to read it. It turned out that the big character one stroke in the middle was slightly broken, and the student mistakenly thought it was the character fire, making a big mistake. Isn't it very laughable? In short, the history and geography tests for new students at Wuben Middle School this time found many interesting answers. What is recorded here is only the general outline. Someone felt the lack of common sense among students, so I slightly revealed its end and submitted it to this talk. I hope those who bear the responsibility of education will pay attention to it.

A New Song of Voice

— Wild Rose

Among the new songwriters of our country, Mr. Li Jinhui is recognized as the most popular nationwide. However, Mr. Li's songs are most suitable for young girls and children. For adult men, it will reveal shyness. In addition to Mr. Li, there is also Mr. Du Tingxiu, who has been working hard on Chinese and Western music and has gained extensive knowledge. He can compose new sounds himself and vent his emotions according to the sadness and joy of the music. He also asks famous Confucians to fill in elegant and popular words, creating a unique style. He completely focuses on singing and does not fall into others' traps. Those who listen are all fascinated. I knew Mr. Du's name from the Nanjing Lizi Society. At that time, Mr. Du was serving as an officer of the society and was praised by famous figures in the Party and state. Scholars called him learned and talented. Previously, I read in newspapers that the Da Zhonghua Company published and issued Mr. Du's new song records. I was very happy that this musician could show off his ambitions, so I bought a set and listened to it first. I only felt that the sound was sonorous, the lyrics were concise, the strings and bamboo were melodious, and the meaning was superb. It can reveal the emotions emanating from the heart. Compared with the popular tunes of the time, such as the zither and the erhu, it has a different flavor. I believe it can be passed down. Also, Mr. Du has been influenced by Christianity for a long time. He deeply regrets that there are no records of hymns in our country. He specially hired the famous pianist Mr. Du Lihua from Qingdao to accompany him. At the same time, he recorded many hymns, which is also a unique masterpiece.

Crying for Tang Yulu

— Yan Enchun

I knew you were talented at fourteen. You were already outstanding in your youthful exuberance. People likened you to Wang Yi-fu upon first seeing you, saying you were a golden boy descended from the heavens. We shared the same hall with hundreds of others for three years. Only you, me, and Yuanlong remained. (Chen Yuanlong's misfortune with the Pujji steamboat happened fourteen years ago.) Now, I am but a traveler in a blue shirt, weeping in the autumn wind and rain.

Like Su Shi returning from overseas on a raft, we parted ways, each flying like swallows in different directions. I saw you briefly in front of the Fragrant Snow screen last year (I met you and Zhimo at the Shanghai Puyi Institute Art Exhibition last year. We exchanged a few words and then parted). Today, I linger dazedly under the moon.

To serve the country and sacrifice yourself was always your ambition. It is most pitiable to hear the market's confusion and hearsay. A dignified secretary of the Ministry of Finance, overturned and wrongly reported as Song Ziwen. (Yesterday's newspaper reported that Song Ziwen's secretary, a Mr. Tang, was shot and killed, hence this correction.) (Response)

▲Soliciting Couplets and Giving Books: Zhang Jun Linqiu, from a prominent Wuxing family. His grandfather and father were well-known for their political achievements. Random Talks on American Women's Life (Part 1)

— Ji

Ms. Qian Jianqiu recently returned from the United States. She majored in law at the Northwestern University Graduate School and earned a doctorate. We are not necessarily advocating for degrees, but seeing her sharp, capable, and possessing the spirit of a man, she is indeed a rising force in the Chinese women's community. During a recent meeting, I inquired about the recent situation of the American women's community. She kindly provided a detailed account, supplemented by her classmate, Mr. Huang Biying. Now, I will record it as follows.

▲Dress: American women mostly consider hair to be beautiful. Ordinary women over the age of sixteen like to perm their hair. Those over forty rarely do so. Since perming is so common, it seems to them to be as necessary as a man wearing a suit and tie. Every night before going to bed, they must wash their face with soap, followed by cleansing cream. This cream is volatile and can expand the pores of the hair, removing dirt from within. Then, they apply tissue cream. This is hygiene before bed, not for beauty. In the morning, they wipe it off, apply powder, and rouge. The powder is not limited to white, but also comes in light red, light yellow, and shades similar to the skin tone. These cosmetics are of pure quality and do not harm the skin. Those who are skilled at dressing up prefer products from Paris. Women there all pay attention to dressing up. Otherwise, they think they are being impolite. As for clothes, the latest style is long skirts that reach the ankles. In winter, they prefer black and long sleeves. In summer, they prefer white or various light colors, sleeveless. The fabric is mostly printed. They wear single layers all year round, but the fabric varies in thickness. The waist of the clothes is very narrow, while the chest is wide, making them easy to wear. The clothes and skirts are connected and without collars. They must wear a hat when going out. The style of the hat varies, and the color often matches the clothes and shoes. They are always dressed up for going out or attending banquets, but they do not pay attention to dressing up at home for the sake of convenience in doing housework.

▲Diet: American women all like to eat meat. However, in order to maintain their beautiful figure, they are afraid of eating too much fat, which can easily lead to obesity. Therefore, they do not dare to eat too much. They only eat one or two slices of meat per meal. Fish, shrimp, sweet potatoes, and vegetables are common side dishes. In addition, there is a type of canned food called "chop suey," which contains a large amount of meat and is cooked in a delicious way, very much to their liking. These canned goods are mostly made by overseas Chinese in New York and Chicago. They do not know how to cook it themselves. Therefore, overseas Chinese who make canned goods are making three times the profit. The number of these shops is also increasing daily. In addition to three meals a day, they also like to eat fruit, candy, biscuits, and coffee. Many also drink tea. They believe that tea can cleanse the spleen and stomach and remove grease. In the past, Chinese tea sold best in the United States. Now, Japanese tea and Indian tea are also gaining ground. It seems that pure, naturally good Chinese tea cannot compare to artificially selected and processed Japanese tea. It can be seen that no matter what it is, relying solely on the excellence of natural products without adding artificial refinement will easily be eliminated.

Rotary Club Story Series

Women, Women (Part 1)

— Yao Sufeng

(1)

On the day of the closing ceremony, the girls' dormitory lost its usual tranquility. Companions greeted each other, said goodbye, and exchanged gifts, fully expressing the deep same-sex affection of women. Some even cried out loud, like lambs reluctant to leave their former residence and good companions.

But comedies were also being performed everywhere: Miss Wang took down the portrait of Valentino hanging on the wall above her bed and personally delivered it to Miss Pan, saying with a smile, "This is yours, your lover in dreams, I'm returning it to you!" Although Miss Pan's face showed some anger, one hand naturally accepted the portrait.

Also, the doorkeeper of the girls' dormitory, Mother Wang, accepted a two-cent bribe from a male student surnamed Zhu and delivered a sealed brocade box to Miss Xu. Miss Xu opened the box and found ten red eggs. She was furious, but the laughter of many people suppressed her anger. She simply threw the ten red eggs on the ground, which Mother Wang picked up.

In the midst of the chaotic scene, Miss Ding, who was known as the "Queen," was also organizing things on her desk. She remembered that at the beginning of the semester, everything was packed in two suitcases, but after four months, even four suitcases could not hold so many things: not to mention the added clothes, even a set of hair-curling tools and a makeup box for manicures also required more than one suitcase to hold.

Mother Wang suddenly came in and said, "Miss Ding, obviously you are sure 'Is it still that Mr. Zhu from yesterday? Just say I've gone home.'" Miss Ding clearly refused with certainty. Mother Wang obeyed and left.

Before long, Miss Ding had packed everything up: the suitcases were not enough, so she used blankets and mattresses as packages, but even those were not enough, so she had to sacrifice a few picture magazines that she usually kept.

Finally, she left this palace of youth, asked Mother Wang to hire a car, asked Mother Wang to carry the two suitcases, and carried two small bags herself, sending them into the car: there were also two large packages, but two unfamiliar men volunteered to carry them out for her; these two men were also students in the school. It is said that on this day, they came specifically to wait outside the girls' dormitory for the mission of assisting the female students.

On the playground, one could not hear the vigorous sound of ball games, but only two or three male students gathered and lingered on the only road from the girls' dormitory to the school gate. From the smiling voices that assaulted Miss Ding from the car window, she could still vaguely hear their praise for her lofty dignity.
